<!-- First-run safety/contraindication screen -->
<div class="safety-screen" id="safetyScreen" style="display:none;">
  <div class="safety-inner">
    <h2>Before you begin</h2>
    <p>This tool generates AI-powered self-hypnosis sessions with narration, visuals, and audio — all running locally in your browser. It is a <strong>wellness self-help aid</strong>, not therapy or medical treatment. Content is generated by AI and is not reviewed by a human therapist.</p>
    <p style="color:var(--accent);">Please confirm you do not currently have any of these conditions:</p>
    <div class="safety-check"><input type="checkbox" id="sc1"><label for="sc1">Active psychosis, schizophrenia, or severe personality disorder</label></div>
    <div class="safety-check"><input type="checkbox" id="sc2"><label for="sc2">Dissociative Identity Disorder (DID) or severe dissociative symptoms</label></div>
    <div class="safety-check"><input type="checkbox" id="sc3"><label for="sc3">Photosensitive epilepsy or seizure disorder</label></div>
    <div class="safety-check"><input type="checkbox" id="sc4"><label for="sc4">Active suicidal ideation or self-harm</label></div>
    <div class="safety-check"><input type="checkbox" id="sc5"><label for="sc5">Under 18 without a caregiver present</label></div>
    <div class="safety-check"><input type="checkbox" id="sc6"><label for="sc6">Currently intoxicated or under the influence</label></div>
    <p style="margin-top:12px; font-size:0.72rem; color:var(--text-faint);">If any apply, please consult a licensed hypnotherapist rather than using a self-help tool. This screen appears once and can be re-viewed in session history.</p>
    <div style="margin-top:12px;">

<script>
  // ====================================================================
  // IDB STORAGE (ported from Adaptive Session Studio — MIT)
  // Replaces localStorage for reliable persistence
  // ====================================================================
  const IDB_NAME = 'stillness-db';
  const IDB_VER  = 1;
  const IDB_STORE = 'kv';
  let _idb = null;
  let _idbOpenP = null;

  function _openIdb() {
    if (_idb) return Promise.resolve(_idb);
    if (_idbOpenP) return _idbOpenP;
    _idbOpenP = new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const req = indexedDB.open(IDB_NAME, IDB_VER);
      req.onupgradeneeded = e => {
        const db = e.target.result;
        if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains(IDB_STORE)) db.createObjectStore(IDB_STORE);
      };
      req.onsuccess = e => {
        _idb = e.target.result;
        _idb.onclose = () => { _idb = null; _idbOpenP = null; };
        resolve(_idb);
      };
      req.onerror = e => { _idbOpenP = null; reject(e.target.error ?? new Error('IDB open failed')); };
    });
    return _idbOpenP;
  }
  async function idbGet(key) {
    try {
      const db = await _openIdb();
      return await new Promise((res, rej) => {
        const r = db.transaction(IDB_STORE, 'readonly').objectStore(IDB_STORE).get(key);
        r.onsuccess = () => res(r.result ?? null);
        r.onerror = e => rej(e.target.error);
      });
    } catch { return null; }
  }
  async function idbSet(key, value) {
    try {
      const db = await _openIdb();
      await new Promise((res, rej) => {
        const tx = db.transaction(IDB_STORE, 'readwrite');
        tx.objectStore(IDB_STORE).put(value, key);
        tx.oncomplete = res;
        tx.onerror = e => rej(e.target.error);
      });
    } catch {}
  }
  async function idbDel(key) {
    try {
      const db = await _openIdb();
      await new Promise((res, rej) => {
        const tx = db.transaction(IDB_STORE, 'readwrite');
        tx.objectStore(IDB_STORE).delete(key);
        tx.oncomplete = res;
        tx.onerror = e => rej(e.target.error);
      });
    } catch {}
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // TOAST NOTIFICATIONS (ported from Adaptive Session Studio — MIT)
  // Non-blocking replacements for alert()
  // ====================================================================
  const TOAST_ICONS    = { info: 'ℹ', success: '✓', warn: '⚠', error: '✕' };
  const TOAST_DURATION = { info: 3500, success: 3000, warn: 5000, error: 0 };

  function toast(type, message, ms) {
    const container = $('toastContainer');
    if (!container) return;
    const duration = ms !== undefined ? ms : TOAST_DURATION[type] || 3500;
    const el = document.createElement('div');
    el.className = `toast toast-${type}`;
    el.innerHTML = `<span class="toast-icon">${TOAST_ICONS[type] || 'ℹ'}</span><span class="toast-text">${escapeHtml(message)}</span><button class="toast-close">×</button>`;
    el.querySelector('.toast-close').addEventListener('click', () => dismissToast(el));
    if (duration === 0) el.addEventListener('click', () => dismissToast(el));
    container.appendChild(el);
    requestAnimationFrame(() => el.classList.add('show'));
    let timer = null;
    if (duration > 0) timer = setTimeout(() => dismissToast(el), duration);
    function dismissToast(t) { clearTimeout(timer); t.classList.remove('show'); setTimeout(() => t.remove(), 220); }
    return el;
  }
  const notify = {
    info:    (msg, ms) => toast('info', msg, ms),
    success: (msg, ms) => toast('success', msg, ms),
    warn:    (msg, ms) => toast('warn', msg, ms),
    error:   (msg, ms) => toast('error', msg, ms),
  };

  // ====================================================================
  // iOS Safari viewport fix (from Perchance skill reference)
  // ====================================================================
  try {
    const isTouchScreen = window.matchMedia("(pointer: coarse)").matches;
    const isSafari = navigator.vendor?.indexOf('Apple') > -1
      && !navigator.userAgent.includes('CriOS')
      && !navigator.userAgent.includes('FxiOS');
    if (isSafari && window.innerWidth < 800 && isTouchScreen) {
      const viewportMeta = document.querySelector("[name=viewport]");
      if (viewportMeta && !viewportMeta.getAttribute("content").includes("maximum-scale")) {
        viewportMeta.setAttribute("content",
          viewportMeta.getAttribute("content") + ", maximum-scale=1");
      }
    }
  } catch(e) { console.error(e); }

  const PACING_RULES = {

  const TOTAL_STEPS = 5;

    currentStep: 1,
    stepsCompleted: { 1: false, 2: false, 3: false, 4: false, 5: false },
    personas: [],
    selectedPersonaId: 'driver',
    selectedMethodId: 'highway',
    intentionType: 'trigger',
    craftedSuggestion: null,
    fullScript: null,
    parsedScript: null,
    droneEnabled: true,
    soundscape: 'drone',
    length: 'medium',
    voice: null,
    speechRate: 0.65,
    voicePitch: 0.85,
    voiceVolume: 1.0,
    droneVolume: 0.35,
    vizOverride: 'auto',
    hud: { fixationDot: true, textDisplay: true, phaseDots: true, phaseLabel: true, progressBar: true, sessionTime: true, labels: true },
    vizSettings: { speed: 1.0, intensity: 1.0, complexity: 1.0, trail: 0.12 },
    duckingEnabled: true,
    paused: false,
    abortFlag: false,
    editingPersonaId: null,
    personaFilter: 'all',

    _preMood: 5,
    _skippedToScript: false,
    vizSpeed: 1.0,
  };
 
  const PHASE_DURATIONS = {
    micro:  { settling: 15,  induction: 30,  deepener: 15,  work: 60,  emergence: 30 },
    quick:  { settling: 30,  induction: 90,  deepener: 30,  work: 120, emergence: 45 },
    short:  { settling: 60,  induction: 180, deepener: 60,  work: 240, emergence: 60 },
    medium: { settling: 90,  induction: 300, deepener: 180, work: 360, emergence: 90 },
    long:   { settling: 120, induction: 420, deepener: 300, work: 540, emergence: 90 },
  };
 
  const _FALLBACK_PERSONA = { id: 'fallback', name: 'Guide', tagline: '', category: 'contemplative', systemPrompt: '' };
  const _FALLBACK_METHOD = METHODS[0];
  const getMethod = () => METHODS.find(m => m.id === state.selectedMethodId) || _FALLBACK_METHOD;
  const getPersona = () => (state.personas.find(p => p.id === state.selectedPersonaId) || state.personas[0]) ?? _FALLBACK_PERSONA;
  const PERSONA_KEY = 'stillness_personas_v1';

  // IDB-backed storage with localStorage migration
  let _personaCache = null;

  async function _initStorage() {
    // Migrate personas from localStorage → IDB
    _personaCache = await idbGet(PERSONA_KEY);
    if (!_personaCache) {
      try {
        const lsRaw = localStorage.getItem(PERSONA_KEY);
        if (lsRaw) { _personaCache = JSON.parse(lsRaw); await idbSet(PERSONA_KEY, _personaCache); localStorage.removeItem(PERSONA_KEY); }
      } catch {}
    }
    if (!Array.isArray(_personaCache)) _personaCache = [];


    // Persist browser storage so IDB isn't cleared
    if (navigator.storage?.persist) await navigator.storage.persist();
  }

  const loadCustomPersonas = () => _personaCache || [];
  const saveCustomPersonas = arr => { _personaCache = arr; idbSet(PERSONA_KEY, arr); return true; };
  function refreshPersonas() {
    const custom = loadCustomPersonas().map(p => ({ ...p, isCustom: true, category: p.category || 'contemplative' }));
    state.personas = [...BUILTIN_PERSONAS, ...custom];
  }
  const escapeHtml = s => String(s).replace(/[&<>"']/g, c => ({'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;'})[c]);

  // ── Reusable helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────
  const $ = id => document.getElementById(id);

  /** Set button to loading state or restore it */
  function setLoading(btnOrId, loading, originalText) {
    const btn = typeof btnOrId === 'string' ? $(btnOrId) : btnOrId;
    if (!btn) return;
    btn.disabled = loading;
    if (loading) btn.classList.add('loading');
    else { btn.classList.remove('loading'); if (originalText) btn.textContent = originalText; }
  }

  /** Start an elapsed-seconds timer. Returns a stop function. */
  function makeElapsedTimer(callback) {
    const start = Date.now();
    const id = setInterval(() => callback(Math.round((Date.now() - start) / 1000)), 1000);
    return () => clearInterval(id);
  }

  /** Show or hide an element by ID */
  function showEl(id, vis) {
    const el = typeof id === 'string' ? $(id) : id;
    if (el) el.style.display = vis === false ? 'none' : '';
  }

  /** Toggle a play/stop preview button pair. prefix = 'voice'|'sound'|'viz' */
  function togglePreviewBtns(prefix, playing) {
    showEl(prefix + 'PreviewBtn', !playing);
    showEl(prefix + 'StopBtn', playing);
  }
 

  /** Update phase dot indicators: -1=reset, >4=all done, N=active */
  function updatePhaseDots(activeIdx) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.phase-dot').forEach((d, i) => {
      d.classList.remove('active', 'done');
      if (activeIdx >= 0 && i < activeIdx) d.classList.add('done');
      if (i === activeIdx) d.classList.add('active');
      if (activeIdx > 4) d.classList.add('done');
    });
  }

  /** Switch between the three main screens */
  function switchScreen(id) {
    ['setup-wizard', 'session-screen', 'post-screen'].forEach(s => {
      const el = $(s); if (el) el.style.display = s === id ? 'block' : 'none';
    });
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // SETTINGS PERSISTENCE (auto-save/load to localStorage)
  // ====================================================================
  const SETTINGS_KEY = 'stillness_settings_v1';
  const _kv = (typeof root !== 'undefined' && root.kv) ? root.kv : null;
  let _saveTimeout = null;

  function _buildSettingsObj() {
    return {
      selectedPersonaId: state.selectedPersonaId,
      selectedMethodId: state.selectedMethodId,
      intentionType: state.intentionType,
      length: state.length,
      soundscape: state.soundscape,
      droneEnabled: state.droneEnabled,
      duckingEnabled: state.duckingEnabled,
      speechRate: state.speechRate,
      voicePitch: state.voicePitch,
      voiceVolume: state.voiceVolume,
      droneVolume: state.droneVolume,
      vizOverride: state.vizOverride,
      vizSettings: state.vizSettings,
      hud: state.hud,
      personaFilter: state.personaFilter,
      methodFilter: state.methodFilter,
      intentionInput: $('intentionInput')?.value || '',
      userAffirmations: $('userAffirmations')?.value || '',
      voiceName: $('voiceSelect')?.value || '',
    };
  }

  function saveUserSettings() {
    clearTimeout(_saveTimeout);
    _saveTimeout = setTimeout(async () => {
      try {
        const settings = _buildSettingsObj();
        // Primary: Perchance KV storage (cloud-backed, cross-device)
        if (_kv) {
          await _kv.settings.set(SETTINGS_KEY, settings);
        }
        // Fallback: localStorage (local-only, survives page refresh)
        localStorage.setItem(SETTINGS_KEY, JSON.stringify(settings));
      } catch {}
    }, 1500);
  }

  async function loadUserSettings() {
    try {
      let s = null;
      // Try Perchance KV first (cloud-backed)
      if (_kv) {
        try { s = await _kv.settings.get(SETTINGS_KEY); } catch {}
      }
      // Fallback to localStorage
      if (!s) {
        const raw = localStorage.getItem(SETTINGS_KEY);
        if (raw) s = JSON.parse(raw);
      }
      if (!s) return false;

      if (s.selectedPersonaId) state.selectedPersonaId = s.selectedPersonaId;
      if (s.selectedMethodId) state.selectedMethodId = s.selectedMethodId;
      if (s.intentionType) { state.intentionType = s.intentionType; const el = $('intentionType'); if (el) el.value = s.intentionType; }
      if (s.length) { state.length = s.length; const el = $('lengthSelect'); if (el) el.value = s.length; }
      if (s.soundscape) { state.soundscape = s.soundscape; state.droneEnabled = s.soundscape !== 'none'; const el = $('soundscapeSelect'); if (el) el.value = s.soundscape; }
      if (s.speechRate != null) { state.speechRate = s.speechRate; const el = $('speechRate'); if (el) el.value = Math.round(s.speechRate * 100); const v = $('speechRateVal'); if (v) v.textContent = s.speechRate.toFixed(2) + '×'; }
      if (s.voicePitch != null) { state.voicePitch = s.voicePitch; const el = $('voicePitch'); if (el) el.value = Math.round(s.voicePitch * 100); const v = $('voicePitchVal'); if (v) v.textContent = s.voicePitch.toFixed(2); }
      if (s.voiceVolume != null) { state.voiceVolume = s.voiceVolume; const el = $('voiceVolume'); if (el) el.value = Math.round(s.voiceVolume * 100); const v = $('voiceVolVal'); if (v) v.textContent = Math.round(s.voiceVolume * 100); }
      if (s.droneVolume != null) { state.droneVolume = s.droneVolume; const el = $('droneVolume'); if (el) el.value = Math.round(s.droneVolume * 100); const v = $('droneVolVal'); if (v) v.textContent = Math.round(s.droneVolume * 100); }
      if (s.vizOverride) { state.vizOverride = s.vizOverride; const el = $('vizSelect'); if (el) el.value = s.vizOverride; }
      if (s.hud) state.hud = { ...state.hud, ...s.hud };
      if (s.duckingEnabled != null) { state.duckingEnabled = s.duckingEnabled; const el = $('duckingToggle'); if (el) el.checked = s.duckingEnabled; }
      if (s.vizSettings) {
        state.vizSettings = { ...state.vizSettings, ...s.vizSettings };
        const vs = state.vizSettings;
        const speedEl = $('vizSpeed'); if (speedEl) { speedEl.value = Math.round(vs.speed * 100); const v = $('vizSpeedVal'); if (v) v.textContent = vs.speed.toFixed(1) + '×'; }
        const intEl = $('vizIntensity'); if (intEl) { intEl.value = Math.round(vs.intensity * 100); const v = $('vizIntensityVal'); if (v) v.textContent = vs.intensity.toFixed(1) + '×'; }
        const cmpEl = $('vizComplexity'); if (cmpEl) { cmpEl.value = Math.round(vs.complexity * 100); const v = $('vizComplexityVal'); if (v) v.textContent = vs.complexity.toFixed(1) + '×'; }
        const trEl = $('vizTrail'); if (trEl) { trEl.value = Math.round(vs.trail * 100); const v = $('vizTrailVal'); if (v) v.textContent = vs.trail.toFixed(2); }
      }
      // Restore HUD toggle checkboxes
      const hudMap = { fixationDot:'cfgFixationDot', textDisplay:'cfgTextDisplay', phaseDots:'cfgPhaseDots', phaseLabel:'cfgPhaseLabel', progressBar:'cfgProgressBar', sessionTime:'cfgSessionTime', labels:'cfgLabels' };
      for (const [key, elId] of Object.entries(hudMap)) { const el = $(elId); if (el) el.checked = state.hud[key] !== false; }
      // Restore filter tabs
      if (s.personaFilter) state.personaFilter = s.personaFilter;
      if (s.methodFilter) state.methodFilter = s.methodFilter;
      if (s.intentionInput) { const el = $('intentionInput'); if (el) el.value = s.intentionInput; }
      if (s.userAffirmations) { const el = $('userAffirmations'); if (el) el.value = s.userAffirmations; }
      if (s.voiceName) state._savedVoiceName = s.voiceName;
      return true;
    } catch { return false; }
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // USER PROFILE (bio, appearance, goals — for AI personalization)
  // ====================================================================
  const PROFILE_KEY = 'stillness_profile_v1';
  let _profileSaveTimeout = null;

  function getProfile() {
    return {
      name: $('pfName')?.value?.trim() || '',
      pronouns: $('pfPronouns')?.value || '',
      age: $('pfAge')?.value || '',
      experience: $('pfExperience')?.value || 'beginner',
      about: $('pfAbout')?.value?.trim() || '',
      appearance: $('pfAppearance')?.value?.trim() || '',
      goals: $('pfGoals')?.value?.trim() || '',
    };
  }

  function saveProfile() {
    clearTimeout(_profileSaveTimeout);
    _profileSaveTimeout = setTimeout(async () => {
      try {
        const profile = getProfile();
        if (_kv) await _kv.settings.set(PROFILE_KEY, profile);
        localStorage.setItem(PROFILE_KEY, JSON.stringify(profile));
        // Update sidebar display name
        const nameEl = $('sidebarDisplayName');
        if (nameEl) nameEl.textContent = profile.name || 'Practitioner';
      } catch {}
    }, 1000);
  }

  async function loadProfile() {
    try {
      let p = null;
      if (_kv) { try { p = await _kv.settings.get(PROFILE_KEY); } catch {} }
      if (!p) { const raw = localStorage.getItem(PROFILE_KEY); if (raw) p = JSON.parse(raw); }
      if (!p) return;
      if (p.name) { const el = $('pfName'); if (el) el.value = p.name; }
      if (p.pronouns) { const el = $('pfPronouns'); if (el) el.value = p.pronouns; }
      if (p.age) { const el = $('pfAge'); if (el) el.value = p.age; }
      if (p.experience) { const el = $('pfExperience'); if (el) el.value = p.experience; }
      if (p.about) { const el = $('pfAbout'); if (el) el.value = p.about; }
      if (p.appearance) { const el = $('pfAppearance'); if (el) el.value = p.appearance; }
      if (p.goals) { const el = $('pfGoals'); if (el) el.value = p.goals; }
      const nameEl = $('sidebarDisplayName');
      if (nameEl && p.name) nameEl.textContent = p.name;
    } catch {}
  }

  /** Build an AI context string from the user's profile for prompt injection */
  function getProfileContext() {
    const p = getProfile();
    const parts = [];
    if (p.name) parts.push(`The subject's name is ${p.name}.`);
    if (p.pronouns) parts.push(`Pronouns: ${p.pronouns}.`);
    if (p.age) parts.push(`Age range: ${p.age}.`);
    if (p.experience) parts.push(`Experience: ${p.experience}.`);
    if (p.appearance) parts.push(`Appearance: ${p.appearance}.`);
    if (p.goals) parts.push(`Goals: ${p.goals}.`);
    return parts.length > 0 ? '\nSUBJECT PROFILE: ' + parts.join(' ') : '';
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // USAGE ANALYTICS — compact incremental aggregation (O(1) storage)
  // ====================================================================
  const ANALYTICS_KEY = 'stillness_analytics_v1';

  /** Get or initialize the analytics store */
  async function getAnalytics() {
    try {
      const data = await idbGet(ANALYTICS_KEY);
      if (data && data.v === 1) return data;
    } catch {}
    return {
      v: 1,
      // Frequency maps: { id: count }
      p: {},   // persona usage
      m: {},   // method usage
      i: {},   // intention type usage
      s: {},   // soundscape usage
      z: {},   // visual effect usage
      ln: {},  // session length usage
      // Time patterns
      hr: new Array(24).fill(0),  // hourly distribution (0-23)
      dw: new Array(7).fill(0),   // day-of-week (0=Sun..6=Sat)
      // Mood & completion
      mood: { preSum: 0, postSum: 0, deltaSum: 0, n: 0 },
      comp: { total: 0, finished: 0, emergency: 0 },
      dur: { sum: 0, n: 0 },
      // Settings usage (running sums for averages)
      cfg: { rateSum: 0, pitchSum: 0, volSum: 0, droneSum: 0, n: 0 },
      // Feature flags: which features the user has tried
      feat: 0, // bitmask: 1=affirmations 2=programs 4=custom-persona 8=skip-to-script 16=timing-fixer 32=share 64=backup 128=double-induction
      // Timestamp
      ts: Date.now(),
    };
  }

  /** Record a completed session into the analytics store */
  async function recordAnalytics(record, wasEmergency) {
    try {
      const a = await getAnalytics();

      // Frequency tallies (increment counters)
      const inc = (map, key) => { if (key) map[key] = (map[key] || 0) + 1; };
      inc(a.p, record.personaId);
      inc(a.m, record.methodId);
      inc(a.i, record.intention);
      inc(a.s, record.soundscape);
      inc(a.z, state.vizOverride || 'auto');
      inc(a.ln, record.length);

      // Time patterns
      const d = new Date(record.date);
      a.hr[d.getHours()] = (a.hr[d.getHours()] || 0) + 1;
      a.dw[d.getDay()] = (a.dw[d.getDay()] || 0) + 1;

      // Mood tracking
      if (record.preMood != null) {
        a.mood.preSum += record.preMood;
        a.mood.n++;
      }

      // Completion
      a.comp.total++;
      if (wasEmergency) a.comp.emergency++;
      else if (record.completed) a.comp.finished++;

      // Duration
      if (record.durationSec > 0) {
        a.dur.sum += record.durationSec;
        a.dur.n++;
      }

      // Settings averages
      a.cfg.rateSum += (record.speechRate || 0.65);
      a.cfg.pitchSum += (record.voicePitch || 0.85);
      a.cfg.volSum += (record.voiceVolume || 1.0);
      a.cfg.droneSum += (record.droneVolume || 0.35);
      a.cfg.n++;

      a.ts = Date.now();
      await idbSet(ANALYTICS_KEY, a);
    } catch(e) { console.error('Analytics write failed:', e); }
  }

  /** Update post-session mood in analytics */
  async function recordPostMood(postVal) {
    try {
      const a = await getAnalytics();
      a.mood.postSum += postVal;
      a.mood.deltaSum += postVal - (state._preMood || 5);
      await idbSet(ANALYTICS_KEY, a);
    } catch {}
  }

  /** Set a feature-used flag (bitmask) */
  async function markFeatureUsed(bit) {
    try {
      const a = await getAnalytics();
      if (!(a.feat & bit)) {
        a.feat |= bit;
        await idbSet(ANALYTICS_KEY, a);
      }
    } catch {}
  }

  // Feature bit constants
  const FEAT = { AFFIRMATIONS: 1, PROGRAMS: 2, CUSTOM_PERSONA: 4, SKIP_SCRIPT: 8, TIMING_FIX: 16, SHARE: 32, BACKUP: 64, DOUBLE_INDUCT: 128 };

  /** Rebuild analytics from remaining history — called after deletes to keep data consistent */
  async function rebuildAnalytics(historyArr) {
    try {
      const existing = await getAnalytics();
      const feat = existing.feat || 0; // preserve feature flags
      const a = { v: 1, p: {}, m: {}, i: {}, s: {}, z: {}, ln: {},
        hr: new Array(24).fill(0), dw: new Array(7).fill(0),
        mood: { preSum: 0, postSum: 0, deltaSum: 0, n: 0 },
        comp: { total: 0, finished: 0, emergency: 0 },
        dur: { sum: 0, n: 0 }, cfg: { rateSum: 0, pitchSum: 0, volSum: 0, droneSum: 0, n: 0 },
        feat, ts: Date.now() };
      const inc = (map, key) => { if (key) map[key] = (map[key] || 0) + 1; };
      for (const r of historyArr) {
        inc(a.p, r.personaId); inc(a.m, r.methodId); inc(a.i, r.intention);
        inc(a.s, r.soundscape); inc(a.z, r.vizOverride || 'auto'); inc(a.ln, r.length);
        const d = new Date(r.date); a.hr[d.getHours()]++; a.dw[d.getDay()]++;
        if (r.preMood != null) { a.mood.preSum += r.preMood; a.mood.n++; }
        if (r.postMood != null) { a.mood.postSum += r.postMood; a.mood.deltaSum += (r.postMood - (r.preMood || 5)); }
        a.comp.total++; if (r.completed) a.comp.finished++;
        if (r.durationSec > 0) { a.dur.sum += r.durationSec; a.dur.n++; }
        a.cfg.rateSum += (r.speechRate || 0.65); a.cfg.pitchSum += (r.voicePitch || 0.85);
        a.cfg.volSum += (r.voiceVolume || 1.0); a.cfg.droneSum += (r.droneVolume || 0.35); a.cfg.n++;
      }
      await idbSet(ANALYTICS_KEY, a);
    } catch(e) { console.error('Analytics rebuild failed:', e); }
  }

  /** Derive insights from analytics — top preferences, patterns */
  function deriveInsights(a) {
    const topKey = obj => Object.entries(obj).sort((a,b) => b[1] - a[1])[0]?.[0] || null;
    const topN = (obj, n) => Object.entries(obj).sort((a,b) => b[1] - a[1]).slice(0, n).map(e => e[0]);
    const avgMood = a.mood.n > 0 ? (a.mood.preSum / a.mood.n).toFixed(1) : null;
    const avgPost = a.mood.n > 0 && a.mood.postSum > 0 ? (a.mood.postSum / a.mood.n).toFixed(1) : null;
    const avgDelta = a.mood.n > 0 ? (a.mood.deltaSum / a.mood.n).toFixed(1) : null;
    const avgDur = a.dur.n > 0 ? Math.round(a.dur.sum / a.dur.n) : 0;
    const peakHour = a.hr.indexOf(Math.max(...a.hr));
    const peakDay = a.dw.indexOf(Math.max(...a.dw));
    const dayNames = ['Sunday','Monday','Tuesday','Wednesday','Thursday','Friday','Saturday'];
    return {
      favPersona: topKey(a.p), favMethod: topKey(a.m), favSoundscape: topKey(a.s),
      favIntention: topKey(a.i), favViz: topKey(a.z), favLength: topKey(a.ln),
      topPersonas: topN(a.p, 3), topMethods: topN(a.m, 3),
      avgPreMood: avgMood, avgPostMood: avgPost, avgImprovement: avgDelta,
      avgDurationSec: avgDur, completionRate: a.comp.total > 0 ? Math.round(a.comp.finished / a.comp.total * 100) : 0,
      peakHour, peakDayName: dayNames[peakDay] || '—',
      totalSessions: a.comp.total,
      avgSpeechRate: a.cfg.n > 0 ? (a.cfg.rateSum / a.cfg.n).toFixed(2) : null,
      featuresUsed: Object.entries(FEAT).filter(([,bit]) => a.feat & bit).map(([name]) => name.toLowerCase().replace('_',' ')),
    };
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // STEP MANAGEMENT
  // ====================================================================
  function validateStep(n) {
    if (n === 1) return !!getPersona();
    if (n === 2) return !!getMethod();
    if (n === 3) {
      const skipCraft = ['trance', 'sleep'].includes(state.intentionType);
      return !!state.craftedSuggestion || skipCraft;
    }
    if (n === 4) return true;
    if (n === 5) return !!state.fullScript;
    return true;
  }
 
  function goToStep(n) {
    if (n < 1 || n > TOTAL_STEPS) return;
    // Forward direction: validate current step
    if (n > state.currentStep) {
      for (let i = state.currentStep; i < n; i++) {
        if (!validateStep(i)) { return; }
        state.stepsCompleted[i] = true;
      }
    }
    // Going backward from a skip clears the skipped state
    if (n < state.currentStep && state._skippedToScript) {
      state._skippedToScript = false;
    }
    state.currentStep = n;
    // Stop all previews when leaving the Configure step
    if (typeof _stopAllPreviews === 'function') _stopAllPreviews();
    updateStepUI();
    if (n === 4) { renderConfigSummary(); }
    if (n === 5) { refreshSummary(); showEl('generateScriptBtn', true); }
    window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });

    // Accessibility: announce step change and move focus
    const stepNames = { 1: 'Choose Your Guide', 2: 'Choose Your Method', 3: 'Set Your Intention', 4: 'Configure the Session', 5: 'Generate Your Session' };
    const announce = $('ariaStepAnnounce');
    if (announce) announce.textContent = `Step ${n} of ${TOTAL_STEPS}: ${stepNames[n] || ''}`;
    // Move focus to step heading
    const heading = document.querySelector(`.step-content[data-step="${n}"] .step-title`);
    if (heading) { heading.setAttribute('tabindex', '-1'); heading.focus(); }
  }
 
  function updateStepUI() {
    // Content
    document.querySelectorAll('.step-content').forEach(el => {
      el.classList.toggle('active', parseInt(el.dataset.step) === state.currentStep);
    });
    // Stepper circles
    document.querySelectorAll('.step-item').forEach(el => {
      const n = parseInt(el.dataset.step);
      const isSkipped = state._skippedToScript && n < state.currentStep && !state.stepsCompleted[n];
      el.classList.toggle('current', n === state.currentStep);
      el.classList.toggle('completed', n < state.currentStep && !isSkipped);
      el.classList.toggle('skipped', isSkipped);
      el.classList.toggle('clickable', n < state.currentStep && !isSkipped);
    });
    // Connectors
    document.querySelectorAll('.step-connector').forEach(el => {
      const [from] = el.dataset.connector.split('-').map(Number);
      const isSkipped = state._skippedToScript && !state.stepsCompleted[from];
      el.classList.toggle('completed', from < state.currentStep && !isSkipped);
    });
    // Step values under circles — show "Skipped" for bypassed steps
    if (state._skippedToScript) {
      for (let i = 1; i <= 4; i++) {
        const el = $('stepValue' + i);
        if (el && !state.stepsCompleted[i]) el.textContent = 'skipped';
      }
    } else {
      $('stepValue1').textContent = state.stepsCompleted[1] ? getPersona().name : '';
      $('stepValue2').textContent = state.stepsCompleted[2] ? getMethod().name : '';
      let s3 = '';
      if (state.stepsCompleted[3]) {
        if (state.craftedSuggestion) s3 = 'crafted ✓';
        else if (state.intentionType === 'trance') s3 = 'pure trance';
      }
      $('stepValue3').textContent = s3;
      $('stepValue4').textContent = state.stepsCompleted[4] ? state.length : '';
    }
    $('stepValue5').textContent = state.fullScript ? 'ready ✓' : '';
    // Nav
    $('btnBack').hidden = state.currentStep === 1;
    $('btnNext').hidden = state.currentStep === TOTAL_STEPS;
    $('btnNext').disabled = !validateStep(state.currentStep);
    // Skip button — only visible on step 1
    const skipBtn = $('btnSkipToScript');
    if (skipBtn) skipBtn.hidden = state.currentStep !== 1;
  }
 
  function refreshSummary() {
    $('summaryGuide').textContent = getPersona().name;
    $('summaryMethod').textContent = getMethod().name;
    $('summaryLength').textContent = state.length.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + state.length.slice(1);
    const intent = $('intentionInput').value.trim() || '(trance only)';
    $('summaryIntention').textContent = intent.length > 60 ? intent.substring(0, 57) + '...' : intent;
    updateBriefPreview();
  }
 
  // ====================================================================
  // RENDERING
  // ====================================================================
  function renderPersonaGrid() {
    const grid = $('personaGrid');
    grid.innerHTML = '';
    const filtered = state.personaFilter === 'all' ? state.personas : state.personas.filter(p => p.category === state.personaFilter);
    filtered.forEach(p => {
      const card = document.createElement('div');
      card.className = `card category-${p.category || 'contemplative'}` + (p.id === state.selectedPersonaId ? ' selected' : '') + (p.isCustom ? ' is-custom' : '');
      card.innerHTML = `<div class="card-name">${escapeHtml(p.name)}</div><div class="card-tagline">${escapeHtml(p.tagline)}</div>${p.isCustom ? `<div class="card-actions"><button class="card-action-btn" data-action="edit">edit</button><button class="card-action-btn" data-action="delete">×</button></div>` : ''}`;
      card.addEventListener('click', e => {
        if (e.target.dataset.action === 'edit') { e.stopPropagation(); openPersonaEditor(p.id); return; }
        if (e.target.dataset.action === 'delete') { e.stopPropagation(); deletePersona(p.id); return; }
        state.selectedPersonaId = p.id;
        saveUserSettings();
        renderPersonaGrid(); renderPersonaDetail(); hideScript(); updateStepUI();
      });
      grid.appendChild(card);
    });
    const addCard = document.createElement('div');
    addCard.className = 'card add-new';
    addCard.innerHTML = '<span>+ create custom</span>';
    addCard.addEventListener('click', () => openPersonaEditor(null));
    grid.appendChild(addCard);
  }
  function renderPersonaDetail() {
    const p = getPersona();
    const el = $('personaDetail');
    if (!p) { el.innerHTML = ''; return; }
    el.innerHTML = `<div class="detail-title">${escapeHtml(p.name)}</div><div>${escapeHtml(p.systemPrompt)}</div>`;
  }
  function renderMethodGrid() {
    const grid = $('methodGrid');
    grid.innerHTML = '';
    const filtered = state.methodFilter === 'all' ? METHODS : METHODS.filter(m => m.category === state.methodFilter);
    filtered.forEach(m => {
      const card = document.createElement('div');
      card.className = `card category-${m.category}` + (m.id === state.selectedMethodId ? ' selected' : '');
      card.innerHTML = `<div class="card-name">${escapeHtml(m.name)}${m.recommended ? `<span class="card-badge">recommended</span>` : ''}</div><div class="card-tagline">${escapeHtml(m.tagline)}</div><div class="card-tags">${m.tags.map(t => `<span class="card-tag">${escapeHtml(t)}</span>`).join('')}</div>`;
      card.addEventListener('click', () => {
        state.selectedMethodId = m.id;
        saveUserSettings();
        // Update soundscape default when method changes
        state.soundscape = m.drone ? 'drone' : 'none';
        state.droneEnabled = m.drone;
        const ssSelect = $('soundscapeSelect');
        if (ssSelect) ssSelect.value = state.soundscape;
        renderMethodGrid(); renderMethodDetail(); hideScript(); updateStepUI();
      });
      grid.appendChild(card);
    });
  }
  function renderMethodDetail() {
    const m = getMethod();
    const el = $('methodDetail');
    if (!m) { el.innerHTML = ''; return; }
    el.innerHTML = `<div class="detail-title">${escapeHtml(m.name)}</div><div>${escapeHtml(m.detail)}</div>`;
  }
  function updateIntentionHint() {
    const type = $('intentionType').value;
    state.intentionType = type;
    const typeData = INTENTION_TYPES[type];
    $('intentionTypeHint').textContent = typeData ? typeData.hint : '';
    hideCrafted();

    // Types that skip crafting — hide the craft button and intention input
    const skipCraft = ['trance', 'sleep'].includes(type);
    const craftBtn = $('craftBtn');
    const intentionInput = $('intentionInput');
    const intentionLabel = intentionInput?.previousElementSibling;

    if (skipCraft) {
      if (craftBtn) craftBtn.style.display = 'none';
      if (craftBtn?.nextElementSibling) craftBtn.nextElementSibling.style.display = 'none'; // sublabel
      if (intentionInput) intentionInput.style.display = 'none';
      if (intentionLabel) intentionLabel.style.display = 'none';
      showEl('affirmationGroup', false);
    } else {
      if (craftBtn) craftBtn.style.display = '';
      if (craftBtn?.nextElementSibling) craftBtn.nextElementSibling.style.display = '';
      if (intentionInput) intentionInput.style.display = '';
      if (intentionLabel) intentionLabel.style.display = '';
      showEl('affirmationGroup', true);
    }

    updateStepUI();
  }
  function updateBriefPreview() {
    const p = getPersona(); const m = getMethod();
    const intention = $('intentionInput').value.trim() || '[no theme]';
    const el = $('briefPreview');
    if (!p) { el.textContent = ''; return; }
    const action = m.category === 'demonstration' ? `demonstrate the <strong>${escapeHtml(m.name)}</strong> effect` : `use the <strong>${escapeHtml(m.name)}</strong> method`;
    el.innerHTML = `<strong>Hey ${escapeHtml(p.name)}</strong> — ${action} for a <strong>${escapeHtml(state.length)}</strong> session on the theme: <strong>"${escapeHtml(intention)}"</strong>${state.craftedSuggestion ? ' (with the crafted suggestion embedded)' : ''}. Write the full script.`;
  }
 
  // ====================================================================
  // CONFIGURE PANEL (Step 4) — dynamic context rendering
  // ====================================================================
  function renderConfigSummary() {
    const p = getPersona(), m = getMethod();
    const el = $('configSummary');
    if (!el || !p || !m) return;

    // Category badges
    const catColors = {
      contemplative: 'var(--accent)', showman: 'var(--accent-warm)',
      somatic: 'var(--accent-green)', authoritarian: '#d46a6a',
      therapeutic: '#8a9aaa', demonstration: 'var(--accent-purple)',
      rapid: '#d4a74a', advanced: '#e06888',
    };
    const pColor = catColors[p.category] || 'var(--text-dim)';
    const mColor = catColors[m.category] || 'var(--text-dim)';

    el.innerHTML = `
      <div style="display:flex;gap:12px;align-items:flex-start;flex-wrap:wrap;">
        <div style="flex:1;min-width:140px;">
          <div style="font-size:0.62rem;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.1em;color:var(--text-faint);margin-bottom:4px;">guide</div>
          <div style="font-size:0.92rem;color:var(--text);font-weight:500;">${escapeHtml(p.name)}</div>
          <div style="font-size:0.68rem;color:${pColor};margin-top:2px;">${escapeHtml(p.category)}</div>
        </div>
        <div style="flex:1;min-width:140px;">
          <div style="font-size:0.62rem;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.1em;color:var(--text-faint);margin-bottom:4px;">method</div>
          <div style="font-size:0.92rem;color:var(--text);font-weight:500;">${escapeHtml(m.name)}</div>
          <div style="font-size:0.68rem;color:${mColor};margin-top:2px;">${escapeHtml(m.category)}</div>
        </div>
      </div>`;

    // Auto-select recommended soundscape based on method
    const ssSelect = $('soundscapeSelect');
    const ssHint = $('soundscapeHint');
    if (ssSelect && ssHint) {
      // Recommend a soundscape based on method
      const recommendations = {
        highway: 'drone', spiral: 'drone', confusion: 'drone',
        'breath-478': 'none', progressive: 'ocean', ericksonian: 'rain',
        'heartbeat-sync': 'heartbeat', 'floating-body': 'binaural',
        'time-distortion': 'binaural', somnambulism: 'binaural',
        'double-induction': 'brown',
      };
      const rec = recommendations[m.id];
      if (rec && ssSelect.value === state.soundscape) {
        ssSelect.value = rec; state.soundscape = rec; state.droneEnabled = rec !== 'none';
      }
      if (m.drone) ssHint.textContent = `Recommended for ${escapeHtml(m.name)}. Procedurally generated — never loops.`;
      else ssHint.textContent = 'Optional. Procedurally generated — never loops. Use headphones for binaural.';
    }

    // Speed hint based on method category
    const speedHint = $('speechRateHint');
    if (speedHint) {
      if (m.category === 'rapid') speedHint.textContent = 'Rapid methods work well at normal or slightly faster speed.';
      else if (m.category === 'advanced') speedHint.textContent = 'Advanced methods benefit from a slow, deliberate pace.';
      else if (p.category === 'authoritarian') speedHint.textContent = 'Authoritarian guides often work well at a slightly faster pace.';
      else speedHint.textContent = 'Slower is more hypnotic.';
    }

    // Length recommendation hint
    const lengthHint = $('lengthHint');
    if (lengthHint) {
      if (m.category === 'rapid') lengthHint.textContent = 'Rapid methods are designed to be short. "Short" is usually plenty.';
      else if (m.category === 'advanced') lengthHint.textContent = 'Advanced methods benefit from longer sessions to build depth.';
      else if (state.intentionType === 'sleep') lengthHint.textContent = 'Sleep sessions work best at medium or long — give yourself time to drift off.';
      else lengthHint.textContent = '';
    }

    // Warnings for specific combinations
    const warnEl = $('configWarning');
    if (warnEl) {
      const warnings = [];
      if (m.category === 'advanced' && state.length === 'short') {
        warnings.push('Advanced methods may not reach full depth in a short session. Consider medium or long.');
      }
      if (p.category === 'authoritarian' && m.category === 'therapeutic' && m.pacing === 'permissive') {
        warnings.push('An authoritarian guide with a permissive method is an unusual combination. It can work, but the tones may clash.');
      }
      if (state.intentionType === 'sleep') {
        warnings.push('Sleep sessions skip the emergence phase. You will not be re-alerted — the session ends in silence.');
      }
      if (warnings.length) {
        warnEl.style.display = 'block';
        warnEl.innerHTML = '<strong>Note:</strong> ' + warnings.join(' · ');
      } else {
        warnEl.style.display = 'none';
      }
    }
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // VOICES, AUDIO, VISUAL
  // ====================================================================
  function loadVoices() {
    const voices = speechSynthesis.getVoices();
    const select = $('voiceSelect');
    select.innerHTML = '';
    const scored = voices.filter(v => v.lang.startsWith('en')).map(v => {
      let s = 0;
      const n = v.name + ' ' + v.lang;
      if (/neural|natural|online/i.test(n)) s += 100;
      if (/enhanced|premium/i.test(n)) s += 90;
      if (/siri/i.test(n)) s += 85;
      if (/google/i.test(n) && !v.localService) s += 50;
      if (/male/i.test(n) && !/female/i.test(n)) s += 10;
      if (/uk|british|gb/i.test(n)) s += 5;
      if (/daniel|oliver|arthur|james|aaron/i.test(n)) s += 4;
      if (/espeak|compact/i.test(n)) s -= 50;
      if (v.localService) s += 2;
      const tier = s >= 85 ? 'neural' : s >= 50 ? 'cloud' : s > 0 ? 'local' : 'basic';
      return { voice: v, score: s, tier };
    }).sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score);

    // Group by tier
    const tiers = { neural: '★ Neural / Premium', cloud: '● Cloud', local: 'Local', basic: 'Basic' };
    const groups = {};
    scored.forEach(item => {
      if (!groups[item.tier]) groups[item.tier] = [];
      groups[item.tier].push(item);
    });

    let first = true;
    for (const tier of ['neural', 'cloud', 'local', 'basic']) {
      if (!groups[tier] || groups[tier].length === 0) continue;
      const og = document.createElement('optgroup');
      og.label = tiers[tier];
      groups[tier].forEach(item => {
        const opt = document.createElement('option');
        opt.value = item.voice.name;
        opt.textContent = item.voice.name + ' (' + item.voice.lang + ')';
        opt.dataset.tier = tier;
        opt.dataset.local = item.voice.localService ? '1' : '0';
        if (first) { opt.selected = true; first = false; }
        og.appendChild(opt);
      });
      select.appendChild(og);
    }
    // Restore saved voice preference
    if (state._savedVoiceName) {
      const opts = select.querySelectorAll('option');
      for (const opt of opts) {
        if (opt.value === state._savedVoiceName) { select.value = state._savedVoiceName; break; }
      }
    }
    updateVoiceInfo();
  }
  function updateVoiceInfo() {
    const select = $('voiceSelect');
    const info = $('voiceInfo');
    if (!info || !select.selectedOptions[0]) return;
    const opt = select.selectedOptions[0];
    const tier = opt.dataset.tier || 'local';
    const local = opt.dataset.local === '1';
    const labels = { neural: '★ Neural voice — highest quality', cloud: '● Cloud voice — good quality, slight latency', local: 'Local voice — instant, lower quality', basic: 'Basic voice — functional' };
    info.textContent = (labels[tier] || '') + (local ? ' · runs offline' : ' · requires internet');
  }
  if (typeof speechSynthesis !== 'undefined') { loadVoices(); speechSynthesis.onvoiceschanged = loadVoices; }
  const getSelectedVoice = () => { const name = $('voiceSelect').value; return speechSynthesis.getVoices().find(v => v.name === name) || null; };
 
  // ====================================================================
  // SOUNDSCAPE ENGINE — procedural ambient audio (replaces AudioDrone)
  // Recipes from ROADMAP: rain, ocean, fire, bowls, heartbeat, binaural,
  // white/pink/brown noise, plus the original engine drone.
  // ====================================================================
  class SoundscapeEngine {
    constructor() { this.ctx = null; this.master = null; this.compressor = null; this.nodes = []; this.running = false; this.type = 'drone'; this._duckGain = null; }

    async start(volume = 0.35, type = 'drone') {
      if (this.running) await this.stop();
      this.type = type;
      this.ctx = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
      if (this.ctx.state === 'suspended') await this.ctx.resume();

      // Master chain: sceneGain → compressor → destination
      this.compressor = this.ctx.createDynamicsCompressor();
      this.compressor.threshold.value = -18; this.compressor.knee.value = 24;
      this.compressor.ratio.value = 3; this.compressor.attack.value = 0.01; this.compressor.release.value = 0.25;
      this.compressor.connect(this.ctx.destination);
      this._duckGain = this.ctx.createGain(); this._duckGain.gain.value = 1.0;
      this._duckGain.connect(this.compressor);
      this.master = this.ctx.createGain(); this.master.gain.value = 0;
      this.master.connect(this._duckGain);

      const c = this.ctx, m = this.master, ns = this.nodes;
      const mkNoise = (filterType, freq, q) => {
        const buf = c.createBuffer(1, 2 * c.sampleRate, c.sampleRate);
        const d = buf.getChannelData(0); let lo = 0;
        for (let i = 0; i < d.length; i++) {
          const w = Math.random() * 2 - 1;
          if (filterType === 'brown') { d[i] = (lo + 0.02 * w) / 1.02; lo = d[i]; d[i] *= 3.5; }
          else d[i] = w;
        }
        const src = c.createBufferSource(); src.buffer = buf; src.loop = true;
        if (filterType !== 'white' && filterType !== 'brown') {
          const f = c.createBiquadFilter(); f.type = filterType; f.frequency.value = freq || 1000; if (q) f.Q.value = q;
          src.connect(f); ns.push(src, f); return f;
        }
        ns.push(src); return src;
      };
      const mkOsc = (freq, type = 'sine') => { const o = c.createOscillator(); o.type = type; o.frequency.value = freq; ns.push(o); return o; };
      const mkGain = (v) => { const g = c.createGain(); g.gain.value = v; ns.push(g); return g; };
      const connect = (...chain) => { for (let i = 0; i < chain.length - 1; i++) chain[i].connect(chain[i + 1]); };
      const startAll = () => ns.forEach(n => { try { n.start && n.start(); } catch(e) {} });

      if (type === 'drone') {
        const bass = mkOsc(70); const bg = mkGain(0.4); connect(bass, bg, m);
        const harm = mkOsc(141); const hg = mkGain(0.18); connect(harm, hg, m);
        const noise = mkNoise('brown'); const ng = mkGain(0.25); const nf = c.createBiquadFilter(); nf.type = 'lowpass'; nf.frequency.value = 280; ns.push(nf);
        connect(noise, nf, ng, m);
        const lfo = mkOsc(0.07); const lg = mkGain(0.08); connect(lfo, lg); lg.connect(bg.gain);
      } else if (type === 'rain') {
        const bed = mkNoise('bandpass', 1200, 0.8); const bg = mkGain(0.5); connect(bed, bg, m);
        const rumble = mkNoise('brown'); const rf = c.createBiquadFilter(); rf.type = 'lowpass'; rf.frequency.value = 200; ns.push(rf);
        const rg = mkGain(0.08); connect(rumble, rf, rg, m);
        // Droplet scheduler
        const droplet = () => { if (!this.running) return;
          const osc = c.createOscillator(); osc.frequency.value = 2000 + Math.random() * 4000;
          const g = c.createGain(); g.gain.value = 0; osc.connect(g).connect(m);
          const t = c.currentTime; g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t); g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.15 + Math.random() * 0.1, t + 0.005);
          g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + 0.02 + Math.random() * 0.015);
          osc.start(t); osc.stop(t + 0.04);
          setTimeout(droplet, 20 + Math.random() * 60);
        };
        setTimeout(droplet, 500);
      } else if (type === 'ocean') {
        const noise = mkNoise('bandpass', 650, 0.5); const ng = mkGain(0.45);
        const lfo = mkOsc(1 / 11); const lg = mkGain(0.35); connect(lfo, lg); lg.connect(ng.gain);
        connect(noise, ng, m);
        const foam = mkNoise('bandpass', 3000, 1); const fg = mkGain(0.06); connect(foam, fg, m);
      } else if (type === 'fire') {
        const bed = mkNoise('brown'); const bg = mkGain(0.12);
        const bf = c.createBiquadFilter(); bf.type = 'lowpass'; bf.frequency.value = 400; ns.push(bf);
        connect(bed, bf, bg, m);
        const crackle = () => { if (!this.running) return;
          const b = c.createBuffer(1, Math.floor(c.sampleRate * 0.008), c.sampleRate); const d = b.getChannelData(0);
          for (let i = 0; i < d.length; i++) d[i] = (Math.random() * 2 - 1) * (1 - i / d.length);
          const s = c.createBufferSource(); s.buffer = b;
          const f = c.createBiquadFilter(); f.type = 'bandpass'; f.frequency.value = 1500 + Math.random() * 3000; f.Q.value = 2;
          const g = c.createGain(); g.gain.value = 0.15 + Math.random() * 0.2;
          s.connect(f).connect(g).connect(m); s.start();
          setTimeout(crackle, 80 + Math.random() * 300);
        };
        setTimeout(crackle, 200);
      } else if (type === 'bowls') {
        const ratios = [1, 2.02, 3.07, 4.16, 5.38]; const decays = [10, 7, 5, 4, 3];
        const strike = () => { if (!this.running) return;
          const root = 180 + Math.random() * 60;
          ratios.forEach((r, i) => {
            const o = c.createOscillator(); o.frequency.value = root * r;
            const g = c.createGain(); g.gain.value = 0.12 / (i + 1);
            o.connect(g).connect(m); const t = c.currentTime;
            g.gain.setValueAtTime(g.gain.value, t); g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + decays[i]);
            o.start(t); o.stop(t + decays[i] + 0.1);
          });
          setTimeout(strike, 8000 + Math.random() * 12000);
        };
        strike();
      } else if (type === 'heartbeat') {
        const beat = () => { if (!this.running) return;
          [0, 0.14].forEach(delay => {
            const o = c.createOscillator(); o.frequency.value = 55;
            const g = c.createGain(); g.gain.value = 0;
            const f = c.createBiquadFilter(); f.type = 'lowpass'; f.frequency.value = 200;
            o.connect(f).connect(g).connect(m); const t = c.currentTime + delay;
            g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t); g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.5, t + 0.03);
            g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + 0.25);
            o.start(t); o.stop(t + 0.3);
          });
          setTimeout(beat, 1050 + Math.random() * 120);
        };
        beat();
      } else if (type === 'binaural') {
        const carrier = 200, beatHz = 6; // Theta range
        const oL = mkOsc(carrier - beatHz / 2); const oR = mkOsc(carrier + beatHz / 2);
        const gL = mkGain(0.3); const gR = mkGain(0.3);
        const merger = c.createChannelMerger(2); ns.push(merger);
        oL.connect(gL).connect(merger, 0, 0); oR.connect(gR).connect(merger, 0, 1);
        merger.connect(m);
      } else if (type === 'pink' || type === 'brown' || type === 'white') {
        const noise = mkNoise(type === 'pink' ? 'lowpass' : type, type === 'pink' ? 800 : undefined);
        const ng = mkGain(type === 'white' ? 0.15 : 0.35); connect(noise, ng, m);
      } else if (type === 'forest') {
        // Layered: breeze (filtered brown), bird chirps (scheduled sine pips)
        const breeze = mkNoise('lowpass', 500); const bg = mkGain(0.2); connect(breeze, bg, m);
        const chirp = () => {
          if (!this.running) return;
          const o = c.createOscillator(); o.frequency.value = 2200 + Math.random() * 2000;
          const g = c.createGain(); o.connect(g).connect(m);
          const t = c.currentTime + Math.random() * 0.5;
          g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t); g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.08, t + 0.02);
          g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + 0.08 + Math.random() * 0.1);
          o.start(t); o.stop(t + 0.15);
          setTimeout(chirp, 1500 + Math.random() * 4000);
        };
        chirp(); setTimeout(chirp, 800);
      } else if (type === 'stream') {
        // Gentle water: filtered white noise + subtle babble modulation
        const water = mkNoise('bandpass', 1200, 0.5); const wg = mkGain(0.3); connect(water, wg, m);
        const lfo = mkOsc(0.3); const lg = mkGain(100); lfo.connect(lg);
        const wf = c.createBiquadFilter(); wf.type = 'bandpass'; wf.frequency.value = 1200; ns.push(wf);
        lg.connect(wf.frequency); water.connect(wf).connect(wg);
      } else if (type === 'wind') {
        // Gusting wind: brown noise with slow LFO on gain
        const wind = mkNoise('lowpass', 600); const wg = mkGain(0.35); connect(wind, wg, m);
        const lfo = mkOsc(0.08 + Math.random() * 0.04); const lg = mkGain(0.2);
        lfo.connect(lg); lg.connect(wg.gain);
      } else if (type === 'thunder') {
        // Deep rumble base + periodic thunder rolls
        const rumble = mkNoise('lowpass', 120); const rg = mkGain(0.3); connect(rumble, rg, m);
        const rain = mkNoise('highpass', 3000); const raing = mkGain(0.08); connect(rain, raing, m);
        const roll = () => {
          if (!this.running) return;
          const o = mkNoise('lowpass', 80); const g = c.createGain(); o.connect(g).connect(m);
          const t = c.currentTime;
          g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t); g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.5, t + 0.3);
          g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + 3 + Math.random() * 2);
          setTimeout(roll, 8000 + Math.random() * 15000);
        };
        setTimeout(roll, 3000 + Math.random() * 5000);
      } else if (type === 'chimes') {
        // Random tuned sine pips with long decay
        const base = mkNoise('bandpass', 400, 0.3); const bg = mkGain(0.05); connect(base, bg, m);
        const chime = () => {
          if (!this.running) return;
          const freqs = [523, 587, 659, 784, 880, 1047, 1175];
          const f = freqs[Math.floor(Math.random() * freqs.length)];
          const o = c.createOscillator(); o.frequency.value = f; o.type = 'sine';
          const g = c.createGain(); o.connect(g).connect(m);
          const t = c.currentTime;
          g.gain.setValueAtTime(0.15, t); g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + 2 + Math.random() * 2);
          o.start(t); o.stop(t + 4);
          setTimeout(chime, 2000 + Math.random() * 5000);
        };
        chime(); setTimeout(chime, 1200);
      } else if (type === 'cave') {
        // Sparse drips with long reverb/echo
        const bg = mkNoise('bandpass', 120, 0.3); const bgg = mkGain(0.03); connect(bg, bgg, m);
        const drip = () => {
          if (!this.running) return;
          const o = c.createOscillator(); o.frequency.value = 2000 + Math.random() * 2000; o.type = 'sine';
          const g = c.createGain(); o.connect(g).connect(m);
          const t = c.currentTime;
          g.gain.setValueAtTime(0.08, t); g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + 0.8 + Math.random());
          o.start(t); o.stop(t + 2);
          setTimeout(drip, 3000 + Math.random() * 8000);
        };
        drip(); setTimeout(drip, 1500); setTimeout(drip, 4500);
      } else if (type === 'crickets') {
        // Chirping insects — filtered noise bursts at cricket-like rates
        const wind = mkNoise('lowpass', 300); const wg = mkGain(0.04); connect(wind, wg, m);
        const chirp = () => {
          if (!this.running) return;
          const o = c.createOscillator(); o.frequency.value = 4000 + Math.random() * 2000; o.type = 'sine';
          const g = c.createGain(); o.connect(g).connect(m);
          const t = c.currentTime, dur = 0.04 + Math.random() * 0.02;
          const reps = 3 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 4);
          for (let i = 0; i < reps; i++) {
            g.gain.setValueAtTime(0.06, t + i * dur * 2); g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t + i * dur * 2 + dur);
          }
          o.start(t); o.stop(t + reps * dur * 2 + 0.1);
          setTimeout(chirp, 1500 + Math.random() * 4000);
        };
        chirp(); setTimeout(chirp, 800); setTimeout(chirp, 2200);
      } else if (type === 'temple') {
        // Deep bell strikes + sustained tonal drone
        const drone1 = c.createOscillator(); drone1.frequency.value = 110; drone1.type = 'sine';
        const drone2 = c.createOscillator(); drone2.frequency.value = 165; drone2.type = 'triangle';
        const dg1 = mkGain(0.12); const dg2 = mkGain(0.06);
        connect(drone1, dg1, m); connect(drone2, dg2, m);
        this.nodes.push(drone1, drone2);
        const bell = () => {
          if (!this.running) return;
          const f = [220, 277, 330, 440][Math.floor(Math.random() * 4)];
          const o = c.createOscillator(); o.frequency.value = f; o.type = 'sine';
          const g = c.createGain(); o.connect(g).connect(m);
          const t = c.currentTime;
          g.gain.setValueAtTime(0.2, t); g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + 5 + Math.random() * 3);
          o.start(t); o.stop(t + 8);
          setTimeout(bell, 6000 + Math.random() * 10000);
        };
        bell(); setTimeout(bell, 3000);
      } else if (type === 'spaceship') {
        // Low engine hum + subtle sci-fi bleeps
        const eng1 = c.createOscillator(); eng1.frequency.value = 42; eng1.type = 'sawtooth';
        const eng2 = c.createOscillator(); eng2.frequency.value = 43.5; eng2.type = 'sawtooth';
        const lp = c.createBiquadFilter(); lp.type = 'lowpass'; lp.frequency.value = 120;
        const eg1 = mkGain(0.15); const eg2 = mkGain(0.12);
        eng1.connect(eg1).connect(lp).connect(m); eng2.connect(eg2).connect(lp);
        this.nodes.push(eng1, eng2);
        const bleep = () => {
          if (!this.running) return;
          const f = [880, 1320, 1760, 2200][Math.floor(Math.random() * 4)];
          const o = c.createOscillator(); o.frequency.value = f; o.type = 'sine';
          const g = c.createGain(); o.connect(g).connect(m);
          const t = c.currentTime;
          g.gain.setValueAtTime(0.02, t); g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + 0.15);
          o.start(t); o.stop(t + 0.2);
          setTimeout(bleep, 4000 + Math.random() * 12000);
        };
        bleep(); setTimeout(bleep, 6000);
      }

      startAll();
      this.master.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(volume, this.ctx.currentTime + 4);
      this.running = true;
    }

    setVolume(v) { if (this.master && this.ctx) this.master.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(Math.max(0, v), this.ctx.currentTime + 0.5); }

    // Ducking: called from speakScript to lower ambience during narration
    duck() { if (this._duckGain && this.ctx) this._duckGain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.2, this.ctx.currentTime + 0.4); }
    unduck() { if (this._duckGain && this.ctx) this._duckGain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(1.0, this.ctx.currentTime + 0.8); }

    setPhaseFreq(phase) {
      if (this.type !== 'drone' || !this.ctx) return;
      const freqMap = { settling: 70, induction: 67, deepener: 63, work: 60, emergence: 70 };
      const target = freqMap[phase] || 70;
      if (this.nodes[0]?.frequency) this.nodes[0].frequency.linearRampToValueAtTime(target, this.ctx.currentTime + 4);
      if (this.nodes[2]?.frequency) this.nodes[2].frequency.linearRampToValueAtTime(target * 2.01, this.ctx.currentTime + 4);
    }

    async stop() {
      if (!this.running || !this.ctx) return;
      this.master.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, this.ctx.currentTime + 2);
      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 2100));
      this.nodes.forEach(n => { try { n.stop?.(); n.disconnect?.(); } catch(e) {} });
      try { this.ctx.suspend(); } catch(e) {}
      this.ctx = null; this.master = null; this._duckGain = null; this.compressor = null; this.nodes = []; this.running = false;
    }
  }
  const drone = new SoundscapeEngine();
 
  let highwayRAF = null;
  let vizRAF = null;
  let stageResizeObs = null;

  // ── Canvas Visual Renderers (ported from Adaptive Session Studio — MIT) ──
  function hexToRgb(hex) {
    let h = hex.replace('#','');
    if (h.length === 3) h = h[0]+h[0]+h[1]+h[1]+h[2]+h[2];
    const r = parseInt(h.slice(0,2),16), g = parseInt(h.slice(2,4),16), b = parseInt(h.slice(4,6),16);
    return `${Number.isFinite(r)?r:128},${Number.isFinite(g)?g:128},${Number.isFinite(b)?b:128}`;
  }

  function renderTunnel(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, rgb = hexToRgb(color), maxR = Math.hypot(cx,cy)*1.1, RINGS = 18;
    ctx.fillStyle = '#000'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    for (let i = RINGS; i >= 0; i--) {
      const frac = ((i/RINGS) + (t*0.18)) % 1, r = frac*maxR, alpha = (1-frac)*0.65+0.05;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx,cy,r,0,Math.PI*2);
      ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},${alpha})`; ctx.lineWidth = 1.5+(1-frac)*3; ctx.stroke();
    }
    const g = ctx.createRadialGradient(cx,cy,0,cx,cy,maxR*0.15);
    g.addColorStop(0,`rgba(${rgb},0.7)`); g.addColorStop(1,`rgba(${rgb},0)`);
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx,cy,maxR*0.15,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fillStyle = g; ctx.fill();
  }

  function renderPendulumViz(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, rx = W*0.38, ry = H*0.38, rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.18)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    ctx.beginPath();
    for (let i = 0; i <= 2400; i++) {
      const frac = i/2400, s = (t - frac*4);
      const x = cx + rx*Math.sin(s*1.23+0.4)*Math.cos(s*0.71);
      const y = cy + ry*Math.sin(s*0.97+1.1)*Math.cos(s*1.03);
      i===0 ? ctx.moveTo(x,y) : ctx.lineTo(x,y);
    }
    ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},0.6)`; ctx.lineWidth = 1.2; ctx.stroke();
  }

  function renderVortex(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, rgb = hexToRgb(color), maxR = Math.min(W,H)*0.44, ARMS = 6;
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.12)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    for (let arm = 0; arm < ARMS; arm++) {
      const baseAngle = (arm/ARMS)*Math.PI*2 + t*0.6;
      ctx.beginPath();
      for (let i = 0; i <= 300; i++) {
        const frac = i/300, angle = baseAngle + frac*Math.PI*3;
        const r = frac * maxR * (0.8 + 0.2*Math.sin(t*1.5+arm));
        const x = cx + r*Math.cos(angle), y = cy + r*Math.sin(angle);
        i===0 ? ctx.moveTo(x,y) : ctx.lineTo(x,y);
      }
      ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},${0.35+0.25*Math.sin(t+arm)})`; ctx.lineWidth = 1; ctx.stroke();
    }
  }

  function renderMandala(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, petals = 8, rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.06)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},0.7)`; ctx.shadowColor = color; ctx.shadowBlur = 12;
    for (let layer = 0; layer < 4; layer++) {
      const R = (layer+1)*Math.min(W,H)*0.1;
      const spin = t*(layer%2===0 ? 0.2 : -0.15) + layer*0.4;
      ctx.globalAlpha = 0.6-layer*0.1; ctx.lineWidth = 1.8-layer*0.3;
      for (let p = 0; p < petals; p++) {
        const base = (p/petals)*Math.PI*2 + spin, tip = base + Math.PI/petals;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(cx,cy);
        ctx.quadraticCurveTo(cx+R*1.5*Math.cos(base+0.3),cy+R*1.5*Math.sin(base+0.3),cx+R*Math.cos(tip),cy+R*Math.sin(tip));
        ctx.stroke();
      }
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx,cy,R*0.4,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.stroke();
    }
    ctx.globalAlpha = 1; ctx.shadowBlur = 0;
  }

  function renderLissajous(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, R = Math.min(W,H)*0.42, rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},0.85)`; ctx.lineWidth = 1.8;
    ctx.shadowColor = color; ctx.shadowBlur = 10;
    const a = 3, b = 2, delta = t*0.4;
    ctx.beginPath();
    for (let i = 0; i <= 600; i++) {
      const th = (i/600)*Math.PI*2;
      const x = cx + R*Math.sin(a*th+delta), y = cy + R*Math.sin(b*th);
      i===0 ? ctx.moveTo(x,y) : ctx.lineTo(x,y);
    }
    ctx.stroke();
    ctx.globalAlpha = 0.08; ctx.fillStyle = '#000'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    ctx.globalAlpha = 1; ctx.shadowBlur = 0;
  }

  function renderColorWash(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const hue = (t*12 + parseInt(color.replace('#',''),16)%360) % 360, hue2 = (hue+40)%360;
    const grad = ctx.createRadialGradient(W*0.4,H*0.4,0,W/2,H/2,Math.max(W,H)*0.7);
    grad.addColorStop(0,`hsla(${hue},70%,35%,1)`);
    grad.addColorStop(0.5,`hsla(${hue2},60%,20%,1)`);
    grad.addColorStop(1,`hsla(${(hue+180)%360},50%,8%,1)`);
    ctx.fillStyle = grad; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    const vig = ctx.createRadialGradient(W/2,H/2,H*0.2,W/2,H/2,H*0.75);
    vig.addColorStop(0,'transparent'); vig.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0.5)');
    ctx.fillStyle = vig; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
  }

  function renderCanvasPulse(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, rgb = hexToRgb(color), maxR = Math.min(W,H)*0.46;
    ctx.fillStyle = '#000'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
      const phase = (t*0.45 + i/6) % 1, r = phase*maxR, alpha = (1-phase)*0.7;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx,cy,r,0,Math.PI*2);
      ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},${alpha})`; ctx.lineWidth = 2+(1-phase)*5; ctx.stroke();
    }
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx,cy,10+4*Math.sin(t*3),0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(${rgb},0.85)`; ctx.fill();
  }

  // Breathing circle — the single most evidence-based hypnotic visual
  function renderBreathingCircle(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, maxR = Math.min(W,H)*0.38, rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    // 4-7-8 cycle: 4s inhale, 7s hold, 8s exhale = 19s total
    const cycle = 19, phase = t % cycle;
    // Haptic at cycle start (once per 19s)
    if (phase < 0.05 && t > 0.1) vibrateBreath();
    let frac; // 0-1 breath position
    if (phase < 4) frac = phase / 4; // inhale: expand
    else if (phase < 11) frac = 1; // hold: full
    else frac = 1 - (phase - 11) / 8; // exhale: contract
    frac = frac * frac * (3 - 2 * frac); // smoothstep ease

    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.12)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    const r = maxR * 0.3 + maxR * 0.7 * frac;

    // Concentric rings at phase offsets
    for (let ring = 4; ring >= 0; ring--) {
      const ringFrac = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, frac - ring * 0.04));
      const rr = maxR * 0.3 + maxR * 0.7 * ringFrac * (3 - 2 * ringFrac);
      const alpha = 0.08 + ring * 0.04;
      // Color shift: cool blue inhale → warm amber exhale
      const hue = 210 - frac * 30; // 210 (blue) → 180 (teal) at full
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx, cy, rr, 0, Math.PI*2);
      ctx.strokeStyle = `hsla(${hue}, 50%, 60%, ${alpha})`; ctx.lineWidth = 1.5; ctx.stroke();
    }

    // Main circle
    const mainHue = 210 - frac * 40;
    const grad = ctx.createRadialGradient(cx, cy, r * 0.3, cx, cy, r);
    grad.addColorStop(0, `hsla(${mainHue}, 55%, 55%, 0.35)`);
    grad.addColorStop(1, `hsla(${mainHue}, 45%, 40%, 0.08)`);
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx, cy, r, 0, Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle = grad; ctx.fill();
    ctx.strokeStyle = `hsla(${mainHue}, 50%, 60%, 0.5)`; ctx.lineWidth = 2; ctx.stroke();

    // Label
    let label = '';
    if (phase < 4) label = 'breathe in';
    else if (phase < 11) label = 'hold';
    else label = 'breathe out';
    ctx.fillStyle = `hsla(${mainHue}, 40%, 70%, 0.6)`;
    ctx.font = '0.8rem -apple-system, sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'center';
    ctx.fillText(label, cx, cy + r + 24);

    // Center dot
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx, cy, 4 + 2 * frac, 0, Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle = `hsla(${mainHue}, 50%, 70%, 0.8)`; ctx.fill();
  }

  // Moiré — historically the most potent trance device (per ROADMAP)
  // Two concentric-ring patterns with one center slowly orbiting the other
  function renderMoire(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, maxR = Math.max(W, H) * 0.8;
    ctx.fillStyle = '#000'; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(136,136,136,0.45)'; ctx.lineWidth = 1;
    // First grating: centered
    for (let r = 6; r < maxR; r += 12) {
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx, cy, r, 0, Math.PI * 2); ctx.stroke();
    }
    // Second grating: orbiting offset
    const ox = cx + Math.cos(t * 0.15) * 18;
    const oy = cy + Math.sin(t * 0.12) * 14;
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(136,136,136,0.4)';
    for (let r = 6; r < maxR; r += 12) {
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(ox, oy, r, 0, Math.PI * 2); ctx.stroke();
    }
    // Soft vignette
    const vig = ctx.createRadialGradient(cx, cy, maxR * 0.2, cx, cy, maxR * 0.6);
    vig.addColorStop(0, 'transparent'); vig.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0,0,0,0.7)');
    ctx.fillStyle = vig; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
  }

  // Starfield warp tunnel — 3D stars projected to 2D with streak lines
  function renderStarfield(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, STARS = 200, focal = 180, rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    if (!renderStarfield._pool) {
      renderStarfield._pool = [];
      for (let i = 0; i < STARS; i++) renderStarfield._pool.push({
        x: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 600, y: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 600,
        z: Math.random() * 600, psx: 0, psy: 0
      });
    }
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)'; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
    const speed = 1.5 + Math.sin(t * 0.3) * 0.5;
    for (const s of renderStarfield._pool) {
      const psx = s.psx, psy = s.psy;
      s.z -= speed;
      if (s.z < 1) { s.x = (Math.random()-0.5)*600; s.y = (Math.random()-0.5)*600; s.z = 600; s.psx = cx; s.psy = cy; continue; }
      const sx = s.x / s.z * focal + cx;
      const sy = s.y / s.z * focal + cy;
      s.psx = sx; s.psy = sy;
      if (sx < 0 || sx > W || sy < 0 || sy > H) continue;
      const brightness = Math.min(1, (600 - s.z) / 400);
      const size = Math.max(0.5, (1 - s.z / 600) * 3);
      ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(${rgb},${brightness})`;
      // Streak line from previous position
      if (psx > 0 && Math.abs(sx - psx) < 40) {
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(psx, psy); ctx.lineTo(sx, sy);
        ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},${brightness * 0.5})`; ctx.lineWidth = size * 0.5; ctx.stroke();
      }
      ctx.fillRect(sx - size/2, sy - size/2, size, size);
    }
  }

  // Candle focal — soft radial glow with position jitter (classic Mesmerist's candle)
  function renderCandle(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H * 0.4, rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.08)'; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
    // Flame jitter
    const jx = cx + (Math.random() - 0.5) * 4;
    const jy = cy + (Math.random() - 0.5) * 3;
    const baseR = 30 + Math.sin(t * 2.5) * 5 + Math.sin(t * 4.1) * 3;
    // Outer glow
    const outer = ctx.createRadialGradient(jx, jy, 0, jx, jy, baseR * 3);
    outer.addColorStop(0, `rgba(${rgb},0.15)`);
    outer.addColorStop(0.4, `rgba(${rgb},0.05)`);
    outer.addColorStop(1, 'transparent');
    ctx.fillStyle = outer; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
    // Inner flame
    const inner = ctx.createRadialGradient(jx, jy - 4, 0, jx, jy, baseR);
    inner.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(255,240,200,0.7)');
    inner.addColorStop(0.3, `rgba(${rgb},0.4)`);
    inner.addColorStop(0.7, `rgba(${rgb},0.08)`);
    inner.addColorStop(1, 'transparent');
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(jx, jy, baseR, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    ctx.fillStyle = inner; ctx.fill();
    // Bright core
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(jx, jy - 2, 4, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,240,0.9)'; ctx.fill();
  }

  // Flow-field particles — simplex noise driven, additive glow
  // Uses a simplified 2D noise (value noise with smoothstep) since we can't import simplex
  function renderFlowField(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    const N = W < 500 ? 250 : 600; // Mobile vs desktop
    if (!renderFlowField._p) {
      renderFlowField._p = [];
      for (let i = 0; i < N; i++) renderFlowField._p.push({ x: Math.random()*W, y: Math.random()*H, px: 0, py: 0 });
    }
    const ps = renderFlowField._p;
    // Resize pool if canvas changed
    if (ps.length < N) while (ps.length < N) ps.push({ x: Math.random()*W, y: Math.random()*H, px: 0, py: 0 });

    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.04)'; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
    ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'lighter';

    const scale = 0.003, speed = 0.5;
    for (const p of ps) {
      p.px = p.x; p.py = p.y;
      // Simple hash-based noise field
      const nx = p.x * scale, ny = p.y * scale, nt = t * 0.08;
      const angle = (Math.sin(nx * 3.1 + nt) + Math.cos(ny * 2.7 - nt * 0.7) + Math.sin((nx + ny) * 1.4 + nt * 0.3)) * Math.PI;
      p.x += Math.cos(angle) * speed;
      p.y += Math.sin(angle) * speed;
      // Wrap around
      if (p.x < 0) p.x += W; if (p.x > W) p.x -= W;
      if (p.y < 0) p.y += H; if (p.y > H) p.y -= H;
      // Draw streak
      const dx = p.x - p.px, dy = p.y - p.py;
      if (Math.abs(dx) < 20 && Math.abs(dy) < 20) {
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(p.px, p.py); ctx.lineTo(p.x, p.y);
        ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},0.3)`; ctx.lineWidth = 0.8; ctx.stroke();
      }
    }
    ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
    // Vignette
    const vig = ctx.createRadialGradient(W/2, H/2, Math.min(W,H)*0.2, W/2, H/2, Math.min(W,H)*0.6);
    vig.addColorStop(0, 'transparent'); vig.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0,0,0,0.4)');
    ctx.fillStyle = vig; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
  }

  // Classic plasma — sum of sines mapped through HSV palette
  function renderPlasma(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    // Render at reduced resolution for performance
    const rW = 192, rH = Math.round(rW * H / W);
    if (!renderPlasma._img || renderPlasma._img.width !== rW) {
      renderPlasma._off = new OffscreenCanvas ? new OffscreenCanvas(rW, rH) : document.createElement('canvas');
      renderPlasma._off.width = rW; renderPlasma._off.height = rH;
      renderPlasma._img = renderPlasma._off.getContext('2d').createImageData(rW, rH);
      // Precompute sine LUT
      renderPlasma._sin = new Float32Array(1024);
      for (let i = 0; i < 1024; i++) renderPlasma._sin[i] = Math.sin(i * Math.PI * 2 / 1024);
    }
    const data = renderPlasma._img.data, sinLut = renderPlasma._sin;
    const S = v => sinLut[((v % 1024) + 1024) % 1024 | 0];

    for (let y = 0; y < rH; y++) {
      for (let x = 0; x < rW; x++) {
        const v = S(x * 3 + t * 40) + S(y * 4 - t * 30) + S((x + y) * 2 + t * 20) + S(Math.sqrt(x*x + y*y) * 2 - t * 50);
        const hue = ((v + 4) / 8 * 360 + t * 15) % 360;
        // HSV to RGB (S=0.7, V=0.6)
        const c = 0.42, x2 = c * (1 - Math.abs((hue / 60) % 2 - 1));
        let r1=0,g1=0,b1=0;
        const h = Math.floor(hue / 60) % 6;
        if (h===0){r1=c;g1=x2;}else if(h===1){r1=x2;g1=c;}else if(h===2){g1=c;b1=x2;}
        else if(h===3){g1=x2;b1=c;}else if(h===4){r1=x2;b1=c;}else{r1=c;b1=x2;}
        const m = 0.18;
        const idx = (y * rW + x) * 4;
        data[idx] = (r1+m)*255; data[idx+1] = (g1+m)*255; data[idx+2] = (b1+m)*255; data[idx+3] = 255;
      }
    }
    const offCtx = renderPlasma._off.getContext('2d');
    offCtx.putImageData(renderPlasma._img, 0, 0);
    ctx.imageSmoothingEnabled = true;
    ctx.drawImage(renderPlasma._off, 0, 0, W, H);
  }

  // Kaleidoscope — wraps any sub-renderer with N-fold mirror symmetry
  function makeKaleidoscope(subRenderer, folds = 6) {
    return function(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
      const cx = W/2, cy = H/2;
      // Render sub-effect to an offscreen canvas
      if (!makeKaleidoscope._off || makeKaleidoscope._off.width !== W) {
        makeKaleidoscope._off = document.createElement('canvas');
        makeKaleidoscope._off.width = W; makeKaleidoscope._off.height = H;
      }
      const offCtx = makeKaleidoscope._off.getContext('2d');
      subRenderer(offCtx, W, H, t, color);
      // Draw N wedges with alternating mirrors
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, W, H);
      const wedgeAngle = Math.PI * 2 / folds;
      for (let i = 0; i < folds; i++) {
        ctx.save();
        ctx.translate(cx, cy);
        ctx.rotate(wedgeAngle * i);
        if (i % 2 === 1) ctx.scale(-1, 1); // Mirror alternate wedges
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(0, 0);
        ctx.lineTo(Math.max(W, H), 0);
        ctx.arc(0, 0, Math.max(W, H), 0, wedgeAngle);
        ctx.closePath();
        ctx.clip();
        ctx.translate(-cx, -cy);
        ctx.drawImage(makeKaleidoscope._off, 0, 0);
        ctx.restore();
      }
    };
  }

  const VIZ_RENDERERS = {
    tunnel: renderTunnel,
    'pendulum-viz': renderPendulumViz,
    vortex: renderVortex,
    mandala: renderMandala,
    lissajous: renderLissajous,
    colorwash: renderColorWash,
    'canvas-pulse': renderCanvasPulse,
    breathing: renderBreathingCircle,
    moire: renderMoire,
    starfield: renderStarfield,
    candle: renderCandle,
    flowfield: renderFlowField,
    plasma: renderPlasma,
    'kaleidoscope-flow': makeKaleidoscope(renderFlowField, 6),
    'kaleidoscope-plasma': makeKaleidoscope(renderPlasma, 8),
  };

  // Phase-based speed multipliers for visuals
  const PHASE_VIZ_SPEED = { settling: 0.5, induction: 1.0, deepener: 0.7, work: 0.9, emergence: 0.6 };

  // ====================================================================
  // PREVIEW ENGINES (Configure tab — separate from session playback)
  // ====================================================================

  // Soundscape preview — uses a separate SoundscapeEngine instance
  const _previewDrone = new SoundscapeEngine();
  let _previewDroneTimeout = null;

  async function previewSoundscape() {
    const type = $('soundscapeSelect')?.value;
    if (!type || type === 'none') { notify.info('Select a soundscape first.'); return; }
    await stopSoundscapePreview();
    try {
      await _previewDrone.start(state.droneVolume, type);
      togglePreviewBtns('sound', true);
      
      $('soundPreviewHint').textContent = 'playing ' + type + '...';
      // Auto-stop after 10 seconds
      _previewDroneTimeout = setTimeout(() => stopSoundscapePreview(), 10000);
    } catch(e) { notify.warn('Could not start audio preview.'); }
  }

  async function stopSoundscapePreview() {
    clearTimeout(_previewDroneTimeout);
    await _previewDrone.stop();
    togglePreviewBtns('sound', false);
    
    $('soundPreviewHint').textContent = 'Listen to a 10-second preview.';
  }

  // Viz preview — renders to the mini canvas with its own rAF loop
  let _vizPreviewRaf = null;
  let _vizPreviewStart = 0;

  function startVizPreview() {
    stopVizPreview();
    const sel = $('vizSelect')?.value;
    const vizKey = sel === 'auto' ? (getMethod().visual) : sel;
    const renderer = VIZ_RENDERERS[vizKey];
    if (!renderer) {
      // Non-canvas types (highway, spiral, pulse, none) — show a label instead
      const wrap = $('vizPreviewWrap');
      if (wrap) { wrap.style.display = 'block'; }
      const canvas = $('vizPreviewCanvas');
      if (canvas) { const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d'); ctx.fillStyle = '#000'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,canvas.width,canvas.height); ctx.fillStyle = '#4a6a84'; ctx.font = '13px -apple-system, sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'center'; ctx.fillText(vizKey === 'none' ? 'Black screen — no visual' : vizKey + ' (non-canvas preview)', canvas.width/2, canvas.height/2); }
      $('vizPreviewLabel').textContent = vizKey;
      togglePreviewBtns('viz', true);
      
      return;
    }

    const wrap = $('vizPreviewWrap');
    const canvas = $('vizPreviewCanvas');
    if (!wrap || !canvas) return;
    wrap.style.display = 'block';
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth || 300;
    canvas.height = 120;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d', { alpha: false });
    const color = '#6b94b8';
    _vizPreviewStart = performance.now();
    $('vizPreviewLabel').textContent = vizKey;
    togglePreviewBtns('viz', true);
    

    function frame() {
      const t = ((performance.now() - _vizPreviewStart) / 1000) * (state.vizSettings.speed || 1.0);
      try { renderer(ctx, canvas.width, canvas.height, t, color); } catch(e) {}
      _vizPreviewRaf = requestAnimationFrame(frame);
    }
