    _vizPreviewRaf = requestAnimationFrame(frame);
  }

  function stopVizPreview() {
    if (_vizPreviewRaf) { cancelAnimationFrame(_vizPreviewRaf); _vizPreviewRaf = null; }
    const wrap = $('vizPreviewWrap');
    if (wrap) wrap.style.display = 'none';
    togglePreviewBtns('viz', false);
    
  }

  // Voice preview state
  let _voicePreviewing = false;

  function setupVisual(visualType) {
    const stage = $('stage');
    // Clean up previous visuals
    if (vizRAF) { cancelAnimationFrame(vizRAF); vizRAF = null; }
    if (highwayRAF) { cancelAnimationFrame(highwayRAF); highwayRAF = null; }
    if (stageResizeObs) { stageResizeObs.disconnect(); stageResizeObs = null; }
    Array.from(stage.children).forEach(c => {
      if (!c.classList.contains('fixation-dot') && !c.classList.contains('audio-indicator')
        && !c.classList.contains('persona-indicator') && !c.classList.contains('method-indicator')
        && !c.classList.contains('session-progress-wrap')) c.remove();
    });

    // Canvas-based renderer (new visual types)
    const renderer = VIZ_RENDERERS[visualType];
    if (renderer) {
      const canvas = document.createElement('canvas'); canvas.className = 'highway-canvas';
      canvas.width = stage.clientWidth; canvas.height = stage.clientHeight;
      stage.insertBefore(canvas, stage.firstChild);
      const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
      const color = getComputedStyle(document.documentElement).getPropertyValue('--accent').trim() || '#6b94b8';
      // Resize observer
      stageResizeObs = new ResizeObserver(() => { canvas.width = stage.clientWidth; canvas.height = stage.clientHeight; });
      stageResizeObs.observe(stage);
      (function draw(ts) {
        if (state.abortFlag) return;
        const speed = (PHASE_VIZ_SPEED[state._currentPhase] || 1.0) * (state.vizSettings.speed || 1.0);
        renderer(ctx, canvas.width, canvas.height, (ts/1000)*speed, color);
        vizRAF = requestAnimationFrame(draw);
      })(0);
      return;
    }

    if (visualType === 'highway') {
      const canvas = document.createElement('canvas'); canvas.className = 'highway-canvas';
      canvas.width = stage.clientWidth; canvas.height = stage.clientHeight;
      stage.insertBefore(canvas, stage.firstChild);
      const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
      // Resize observer
      stageResizeObs = new ResizeObserver(() => { canvas.width = stage.clientWidth; canvas.height = stage.clientHeight; });
      stageResizeObs.observe(stage);
      const lines = []; for (let i = 0; i < 8; i++) lines.push({ y: (canvas.height / 8) * i, speed: 1.2 + Math.random() * 0.4 });
      (function draw() {
        if (state.abortFlag) return;
        const W = canvas.width, H = canvas.height;
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.18)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
        ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(212,220,232,0.55)'; ctx.lineWidth = 4;
        lines.forEach(l => { l.y += l.speed; if (l.y > H + 40) l.y = -40; ctx.globalAlpha = Math.min(1,(l.y/H)*1.2)*0.7; ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(W/2, l.y); ctx.lineTo(W/2, l.y+28); ctx.stroke(); });
        ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
        const g = ctx.createRadialGradient(W/2, H*0.38, 20, W/2, H*0.38, H*0.5); g.addColorStop(0,'rgba(0,0,0,0)'); g.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0.5)');
        ctx.fillStyle = g; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
        highwayRAF = requestAnimationFrame(draw);
      })();
    } else if (visualType === 'spiral') {
      const svg = document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg','svg');
      svg.setAttribute('class','spiral-svg'); svg.setAttribute('viewBox','0 0 100 100');
      let d = 'M 50 50 ';
      for (let t=0;t<30;t+=0.1) { const r=0.5*t; d += `L ${(50+r*Math.cos(t)).toFixed(2)} ${(50+r*Math.sin(t)).toFixed(2)} `; }
      const p = document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg','path');
      p.setAttribute('d',d); p.setAttribute('stroke','rgba(107,148,184,0.4)'); p.setAttribute('stroke-width','0.4'); p.setAttribute('fill','none');
      svg.appendChild(p); stage.insertBefore(svg, stage.firstChild);
    } else {
      // Default: CSS pulse rings
      const wrap = document.createElement('div'); wrap.className = 'pulse-rings';
      for (let i = 0; i < 3; i++) { const r = document.createElement('div'); r.className = 'pulse-ring'; wrap.appendChild(r); }
      stage.insertBefore(wrap, stage.firstChild);
    }
  }
  const stopVisuals = () => {
    if (highwayRAF) cancelAnimationFrame(highwayRAF); highwayRAF = null;
    if (vizRAF) cancelAnimationFrame(vizRAF); vizRAF = null;
    if (stageResizeObs) { stageResizeObs.disconnect(); stageResizeObs = null; }
  };
 
  // ====================================================================
  // PERSONA EDITOR
  // ====================================================================
  function openPersonaEditor(id) {
    state.editingPersonaId = id;
    $('personaModalTitle').textContent = id ? 'edit persona' : 'create custom persona';
    if (id) {
      const p = state.personas.find(x => x.id === id);
      $('personaFormName').value = p.name;
      $('personaFormTagline').value = p.tagline;
      $('personaFormPrompt').value = p.systemPrompt;
      $('personaFormCategory').value = p.category || 'contemplative';
    } else {
      $('personaFormName').value = '';
      $('personaFormTagline').value = '';
      $('personaFormPrompt').value = '';
      $('personaFormCategory').value = 'contemplative';
    }
    $('personaModal').classList.add('visible');
  }
  const closePersonaEditor = () => { $('personaModal').classList.remove('visible'); state.editingPersonaId = null; };
  function savePersonaFromForm() {
    const name = $('personaFormName').value.trim();
    const tagline = $('personaFormTagline').value.trim();
    const systemPrompt = $('personaFormPrompt').value.trim();
    const category = $('personaFormCategory').value || 'contemplative';
    if (!name || !systemPrompt) { notify.warn('Name and voice instruction required.'); return; }
    let custom = loadCustomPersonas();
    if (state.editingPersonaId) {
      custom = custom.map(p => p.id === state.editingPersonaId ? { ...p, name, tagline, systemPrompt, category } : p);
    } else {
      const id = 'custom_' + Date.now();
      custom.push({ id, name, tagline: tagline || '(custom)', systemPrompt, category });
      state.selectedPersonaId = id;
    }
    if (!saveCustomPersonas(custom)) { notify.error('Could not save: browser storage may be full.'); return; }
    refreshPersonas(); renderPersonaGrid(); renderPersonaDetail(); closePersonaEditor();
  }
  function deletePersona(id) {
    if (!confirm('Delete this persona?')) return;
    saveCustomPersonas(loadCustomPersonas().filter(p => p.id !== id));
    if (state.selectedPersonaId === id) state.selectedPersonaId = 'driver';
    refreshPersonas(); renderPersonaGrid(); renderPersonaDetail();
  }
 
  // ====================================================================
  // CRAFTER
  // ====================================================================
  let _aiInProgress = false; // Prevents double-click firing two concurrent AI calls

  async function craftSuggestion() {
    if (_aiInProgress) { notify.info('An AI call is already in progress.'); return; }
    const rough = $('intentionInput').value.trim();
    const skipTypes = ['trance', 'sleep'];
    if (!rough && !skipTypes.includes(state.intentionType)) { notify.warn('Describe what you want first.'); return; }
    const type = INTENTION_TYPES[state.intentionType];
    if (!type) { notify.warn('Select an intention type first.'); return; }
    _aiInProgress = true;
    const progressLabel = $('craftProgressLabel');
    setLoading('craftBtn', true);
    setLoading('recraftBtn', true);
    $('craftProgress').classList.add('visible');
    progressLabel.textContent = 'crafting your suggestion — about 2–3 minutes...';
    const stopTimer = makeElapsedTimer(s => { progressLabel.textContent = `crafting... ${s}s elapsed`; });

    const instruction = `You are a master hypnotherapist converting a user's rough intention into a technically-precise hypnotic suggestion.

TYPE: ${type.label}
USER'S ROUGH DESCRIPTION: "${rough}"

UNIVERSAL RULES:
• Second person ("you")
• Presupposition ("you'll notice" not "you will feel") [For convincer/novelty: direct present-tense fine]
• Somatic anchoring (tie states to physical sensations)
• Automaticity ("automatically", "without effort")
• Progressive intensification
• Future-pacing ("from now on")
• Positive construction only
• Specificity

TYPE-SPECIFIC GUIDANCE:
${type.guidance}
${getProfileContext()}
Output EXACTLY this JSON, no other text, no markdown fences:
{
  "craftedSuggestion": "Complete hypnotic suggestion, 3-5 sentences, ready to deliver verbatim. Second person.",
  "trigger": "Specific trigger phrase, or 'ongoing state'",
  "coreResponse": "Specific response/effect, 3-7 words",
  "reinforcementPhrases": ["Three or four short variants (5-10 words)"],
  "explanation": "ONE sentence on the technique used"
}`;

    try {
      const data = await root.aiTextPlugin({ instruction, startWith: '{', stopSequences: ['\n\n\n'], hideStartWith: true });
      if (data.stopReason === 'error') throw new Error('AI generation encountered an error.');
      let text = (data.generatedText || '').trim();
      if (!text.startsWith('{')) text = '{' + text;
      const lb = text.lastIndexOf('}'); if (lb > -1) text = text.substring(0, lb + 1);
      state.craftedSuggestion = JSON.parse(text);
      showCrafted();
      updateStepUI();
      notify.success('Suggestion crafted successfully.');
    } catch (e) { console.error(e); notify.warn('Crafting failed: ' + e.message + '. Try again.'); }
    finally {
      _aiInProgress = false;
      stopTimer();
      setLoading('craftBtn', false, 'craft hypnotic suggestion →');
      setLoading('recraftBtn', false);
      $('craftProgress').classList.remove('visible');
    }
  }
  function showCrafted() {
    const c = state.craftedSuggestion;
    $('craftedText').textContent = c.craftedSuggestion;
    $('craftedText').style.display = 'block';
    $('craftedEditable').style.display = 'none';
    $('saveEditBtn').style.display = 'none';
    $('craftedMeta').innerHTML = `<strong>trigger:</strong> ${escapeHtml(c.trigger||'—')}  ·  <strong>effect:</strong> ${escapeHtml(c.coreResponse||'—')}<br><strong>technique:</strong> ${escapeHtml(c.explanation||'—')}`;
    $('craftedPreview').classList.add('visible');
  }
  function hideCrafted() { state.craftedSuggestion = null; $('craftedPreview').classList.remove('visible'); hideScript(); }
  function toggleEditCrafted() {
    const t = $('craftedText'), e = $('craftedEditable'), s = $('saveEditBtn');
    e.value = state.craftedSuggestion.craftedSuggestion;
    t.style.display = 'none'; e.style.display = 'block'; s.style.display = 'inline-block';
  }
  function saveEditCrafted() {
    state.craftedSuggestion.craftedSuggestion = $('craftedEditable').value.trim();
    showCrafted(); hideScript();
  }
 

  // ====================================================================
  // SCRIPT GEN — per-phase generation with live progress
  // ====================================================================

  /** Determine the phase list based on session length */

  /** Determine the phase list — includes affirmation interludes between work phases */
  function getPhaseList() {
    const base = ['settling', 'induction', 'deepener'];
    const workCount = state.length === 'long' ? 3 : state.length === 'medium' ? 2 : 1;
    const userAff = $('userAffirmations')?.value?.trim();
    for (let i = 1; i <= workCount; i++) {
      // Add affirmation interlude before each work block (if user provided affirmations)
      if (userAff && i > 1) base.push(`affirm-${i}`);
      base.push(workCount > 1 ? `work-${i}` : 'work');
    }
    base.push('emergence');
    return base;
  }

  /** Render phase progress with state: pending, streaming, done, error, warn */
  function renderGenProgress(phases, stateMask, eta, retryCallback) {
    const wrap = $('genProgress');
    const container = $('genPhases');
    const etaEl = $('genEta');
    if (!wrap || !container) return;
    wrap.style.display = 'block';
    const labels = { settling: 'Settling', induction: 'Induction', deepener: 'Deepener', emergence: 'Emergence' };
    container.innerHTML = phases.map((p, i) => {
      const label = labels[p] || (p.startsWith('work') ? 'Work' + (p.includes('-') ? ' ' + p.split('-')[1] : '') : p.startsWith('affirm') ? 'Affirm' : p);
      const st = stateMask[i] || 'pending';
      return `<div class="gen-phase ${st}" data-phase-idx="${i}"><div class="gen-dot"></div><span>${label}</span></div>`;
    }).join('');
    if (etaEl) etaEl.textContent = eta || '';
    // Wire click-to-retry for error/warn states
    if (retryCallback) {
      container.querySelectorAll('.gen-phase.error, .gen-phase.warn').forEach(el => {
        el.addEventListener('click', () => retryCallback(parseInt(el.dataset.phaseIdx)));
      });
    }
  }

  // Generation state held outside so retry can access it
  let _genState = null;

  async function generateFullScript() {
    if (_aiInProgress) { notify.info('An AI call is already in progress.'); return; }
    const editedText = $('scriptText').value.trim();
    if (state.fullScript && editedText && editedText !== state.fullScript.trim()) {
      if (!confirm('Your manual edits to the script will be discarded. Regenerate anyway?')) return;
    }
    _aiInProgress = true;
    const persona = getPersona();
    const method = getMethod();
    const durations = PHASE_DURATIONS[state.length];
    const rough = $('intentionInput').value.trim();
    const wpm = 50;
    const targetWords = Object.fromEntries(Object.entries(durations).map(([k,v]) => [k, Math.round(v * wpm / 60)]));

    setLoading('generateScriptBtn', true);
    setLoading('regenScriptBtn', true);

    const phases = getPhaseList();
    const stateMask = phases.map(() => 'pending');
    const phaseTimes = [];
    const phaseResults = {};

    const craftedBlock = state.craftedSuggestion ? `\nCRAFTED SUGGESTION: "${state.craftedSuggestion.craftedSuggestion}"\nTRIGGER: ${state.craftedSuggestion.trigger}\nEFFECT: ${state.craftedSuggestion.coreResponse}` : '';
    const userAff = $('userAffirmations')?.value?.trim();
    const affirmLines = userAff ? userAff.split('\n').filter(l => l.trim()).map(l => l.trim()) : [];
    const affirmBlock = affirmLines.length ? `\nUSER AFFIRMATIONS:\n${affirmLines.map(l => `"${l}"`).join('\n')}` : '';
    const demoNote = method.category === 'demonstration' ? '\nDEMONSTRATION METHOD: direct suggestions, build effect, include TEST.' : '';

    const profileCtx = getProfileContext();
    const sharedContext = `You are ${persona.name}. ${persona.systemPrompt}\nMETHOD: ${method.name}. ${method.detail}\nPACING: ${PACING_RULES[method.pacing]}\nTHEME: "${rough || 'general trance experience'}"${craftedBlock}${affirmBlock}${demoNote}${profileCtx}`;

    // Phase-specific instructions
    const phaseInstructions = {
      settling: `Write the SETTLING phase (~${targetWords.settling} words). Orient the user. Open naturally — don't say "hello". Use [PAUSE n] markers. Output ONLY the script text.`,
      induction: `Write the INDUCTION phase (~${targetWords.induction} words). Move from awareness toward trance using ${method.name}. Use [PAUSE n] markers. Output ONLY script text.`,
      deepener: `Write the DEEPENER phase (~${targetWords.deepener} words). Take them deeper.${state.craftedSuggestion ? ' Foreshadow the suggestion.' : ''}${affirmLines.length ? ' Begin weaving affirmations.' : ''} Use [PAUSE n]. Output ONLY script text.`,
      emergence: `Write the EMERGENCE phase (~${targetWords.emergence} words). ${method.category === 'demonstration' ? 'FIRST: deliver the TEST. THEN count up 1-5.' : state.craftedSuggestion ? 'State core effect one final time, THEN count up 1-5.' : 'Count up 1-5 to full alertness.'} Use [PAUSE n]. Output ONLY script text.`,
    };

    // Work phase instructions
    const workCount = phases.filter(p => p.startsWith('work')).length;
    const workWordsEach = Math.round(targetWords.work / workCount);
    phases.forEach(p => {
      if (p.startsWith('affirm')) {
        // Affirmation interlude — short, poetic, uses the user's exact words
        phaseInstructions[p] = `Write a brief affirmation interlude (~40-60 words). Deliver these affirmations in ${persona.name}'s voice, woven into flowing, hypnotic language:\n${affirmLines.map(l => `"${l}"`).join('\n')}\nUse the user's exact words. Add [PAUSE 3] between each. Poetic, rhythmic, repetitive. Output ONLY script text.`;
      } else if (p.startsWith('work')) {
        const workIdx = p.includes('-') ? parseInt(p.split('-')[1]) : 1;
        let note = `Write WORK phase ${workIdx} of ${workCount} (~${workWordsEach} words). `;
        if (workIdx === 1) note += state.craftedSuggestion ? 'Deliver the crafted suggestion verbatim. Begin reinforcement.' : method.category === 'demonstration' ? 'BUILD the demonstration effect.' : 'Therapeutic deepening.';
        else if (workIdx === workCount) note += state.craftedSuggestion ? 'Final reinforcement. Peak intensity. Future-pace.' : 'Peak deepening. Consolidation.';
        else note += state.craftedSuggestion ? 'Continue reinforcement with variants. Intensify.' : 'Continue deepening.';
        note += ' Use [PAUSE n]. Output ONLY script text.';
        phaseInstructions[p] = note;
      }
    });

    // Save gen state for retry access
    _genState = { phases, stateMask, phaseResults, phaseTimes, sharedContext, phaseInstructions, persona, method, genStartTime: Date.now(), priorSummary: '' };

    const retryPhase = async (idx) => {
      if (_aiInProgress && !_genState) return;
      const gs = _genState;
      gs.stateMask[idx] = 'streaming';
      renderGenProgress(gs.phases, gs.stateMask, null, retryPhase);
      try {
        const result = await generateSinglePhase(gs, idx);
        gs.phaseResults[gs.phases[idx]] = result;
        gs.stateMask[idx] = 'done';
        renderGenProgress(gs.phases, gs.stateMask, null, retryPhase);
        assembleAndShowScript(gs);
        notify.success(`Phase "${gs.phases[idx]}" regenerated successfully.`);
      } catch (e) {
        gs.stateMask[idx] = 'error';
        renderGenProgress(gs.phases, gs.stateMask, null, retryPhase);
        notify.error(`Retry failed: ${e.message}. Click the red indicator to try again.`);
      }
    };

    // Show initial progress
    renderGenProgress(phases, stateMask, `Estimated: ~${phases.length * 60}s remaining`, retryPhase);
    const genStartTime = Date.now();
    const stopTimer = makeElapsedTimer(s => {
      const avgTime = phaseTimes.length > 0 ? phaseTimes.reduce((a,b) => a+b, 0) / phaseTimes.length : 60;
      const remSec = Math.max(0, Math.round(avgTime * (phases.length - phaseTimes.length)));
      $('genEta').textContent = `${s}s elapsed · ~${remSec}s remaining`;
    });

    try {
      let priorSummary = '';

      for (let i = 0; i < phases.length; i++) {
        const phase = phases[i];
        const phaseStart = Date.now();
        stateMask[i] = 'streaming';
        renderGenProgress(phases, stateMask, null, retryPhase);

        try {
          const result = await generateSinglePhase(_genState, i);
          phaseResults[phase] = result;
          priorSummary += `\n${phase.toUpperCase()}: ${result.length > 200 ? result.substring(0, 150).replace(/\[PAUSE \d+\]/g, '') + '...' : result.replace(/\[PAUSE \d+\]/g, '')}`;
          _genState.priorSummary = priorSummary;
          stateMask[i] = 'done';
          phaseTimes.push((Date.now() - phaseStart) / 1000);
        } catch (e) {
          console.error(`Phase "${phase}" failed:`, e);
          if (e.message.includes('AI') || e.message.includes('error') || e.message.includes('failed')) {
            stateMask[i] = 'error';
            notify.error(`"${phase}" failed: ${e.message}. Click the red indicator to retry.`);
          } else {
            stateMask[i] = 'warn';
            notify.warn(`"${phase}" had an issue: ${e.message}. Click the yellow indicator to retry.`);
          }
          // Continue to next phase — partial script is better than nothing
          phaseTimes.push(60); // estimate for ETA
        }
        renderGenProgress(phases, stateMask, null, retryPhase);
      }

      assembleAndShowScript(_genState);
      const totalTime = Math.round((Date.now() - genStartTime) / 1000);
      const failures = stateMask.filter(s => s === 'error' || s === 'warn').length;
      if (failures > 0) {
        notify.warn(`Script generated in ${totalTime}s with ${failures} phase(s) needing retry. Click indicators to fix.`);
      } else {
        notify.success(`Script generated in ${totalTime}s — ${phases.length} phases complete.`);
      }

    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e);
      notify.error('Script generation failed: ' + e.message);
    } finally {
      _aiInProgress = false;
      stopTimer();
      setLoading('generateScriptBtn', false, 'generate full script');
      setLoading('regenScriptBtn', false);
    }
  }

  /** Generate a single phase via aiTextPlugin */
  async function generateSinglePhase(gs, idx) {
    const phase = gs.phases[idx];
    const summaryBlock = gs.priorSummary ? `\n\nSO FAR (summary — continue seamlessly, DO NOT repeat):\n${gs.priorSummary}` : '';
    const instruction = `${gs.sharedContext}${summaryBlock}\n\n═══ YOUR TASK ═══\n${gs.phaseInstructions[phase]}\n\nStay in ${gs.persona.name}'s voice. Continue naturally. No ===PHASE=== markers. Start immediately:`;

    const data = await root.aiTextPlugin({ instruction, stopSequences: ['\n\n\n\n', '==='], hideStartWith: true });
    if (data.stopReason === 'error') throw new Error('AI returned an error');

    let text = (data.generatedText || '').trim();
    text = text.replace(/^===\w+===\s*/i, '').trim();
    if (!text || text.length < 15) throw new Error('Phase returned too little text');
    return text;
  }

  /** Assemble all completed phases into a full script */
  function assembleAndShowScript(gs) {
    const markerMap = { settling: 'SETTLING', induction: 'INDUCTION', deepener: 'DEEPENER', emergence: 'EMERGENCE' };
    let fullScript = '';
    gs.phases.forEach(p => {
      if (!gs.phaseResults[p]) return; // skip failed phases
      const marker = markerMap[p] || (p.startsWith('affirm') ? 'WORK' : 'WORK');
      fullScript += `===${marker}===\n${gs.phaseResults[p]}\n\n`;
    });
    if (fullScript.trim().length > 50) {
      state.fullScript = fullScript.trim();
      state.parsedScript = parseScript(state.fullScript);
      showScript();
      updateStepUI();
    }
  }


 
  function parseScript(text) {
    const phases = { settling: '', induction: '', deepener: '', work: '', emergence: '' };
    const markers = [
      { key: 'settling', rx: /===\s*SETTLING\s*===/i },
      { key: 'induction', rx: /===\s*INDUCTION\s*===/i },
      { key: 'deepener', rx: /===\s*DEEPENER\s*===/i },
      { key: 'work', rx: /===\s*WORK\s*===/i },
      { key: 'emergence', rx: /===\s*EMERGENCE\s*===/i },
    ];
    const positions = markers.map(m => { const match = text.match(m.rx); return { key: m.key, index: match ? match.index + match[0].length : -1, start: match ? match.index : -1 }; });
    const found = positions.filter(p => p.index !== -1).sort((a,b) => a.index - b.index);
    for (let i = 0; i < found.length; i++) {
      const cur = found[i];
      const end = i + 1 < found.length ? found[i+1].start : text.length;
      phases[cur.key] = text.substring(cur.index, end).trim();
    }
    return phases;
  }
 
  function showScript() {
    _scriptEditedSinceGen = false;
    updateFixTimingsVisibility();
    $('scriptText').value = state.fullScript;
    // Strip phase markers and pause markers before counting actual spoken words
    const spokenOnly = state.fullScript
      .replace(/===\s*\w+\s*===/gi, ' ')
      .replace(/\[PAUSE\s+\d+\]/gi, ' ');
    const words = spokenOnly.split(/\s+/).filter(w => w.length > 0).length;
    const pauses = (state.fullScript.match(/\[PAUSE\s+\d+\]/gi) || []).length;
    const pauseSecs = (state.fullScript.match(/\[PAUSE\s+(\d+)\]/gi) || []).reduce((sum, m) => sum + parseInt(m.match(/\d+/)[0], 10), 0);
    $('scriptStats').innerHTML = `<strong>${words}</strong> words · <strong>${pauses}</strong> pauses (${pauseSecs}s) · estimated: <strong>${Math.round(words / 50 + pauseSecs / 60)} min</strong><br>Edit below before starting.`;
    $('scriptPreview').classList.add('visible');
  }
  function hideScript() { state.fullScript = null; state.parsedScript = null; $('scriptPreview').classList.remove('visible'); updateStepUI(); }

  // ====================================================================
  // SCRIPT TIMING FIXER — recalculates [PAUSE N] markers heuristically
  // ====================================================================
  let _scriptEditedSinceGen = false;

  /** Detect directive phrases that need longer pauses after them */
  const DIRECTIVE_RX = /\b(close your eyes|take a (?:deep )?breath|breathe (?:in|out)|notice|feel|relax|let go|allow|imagine|picture|visualize|focus|drift|sink|float|deeper|sleep now|rest)\b/i;
  const ELLIPSIS_RX = /\.{2,}|…/;

  /**
   * Fix [PAUSE N] timings in a script based on content heuristics.
   * - Removes existing pauses and recalculates
   * - Breaks sentences >30 words at clause boundaries
   * - Combines fragments <3 words with adjacent sentences
   * - Inserts pauses based on content type and length
   */
  function fixScriptTimings(scriptText) {
    const phaseRx = /(===\s*\w+\s*===)/gi;
    const parts = scriptText.split(phaseRx);

    const processed = parts.map((part) => {
      if (/(===\s*\w+\s*===)/i.test(part)) return part;

      let clean = part.replace(/\[PAUSE\s+\d+\]/gi, '').trim();
      if (!clean) return part;

      // Split into raw sentences
      let sentences = clean.split(/(?<=[.!?])\s+/).filter(s => s.trim().length > 0);

      // Break long sentences (>30 words) at clause boundaries
      const broken = [];
      for (const sent of sentences) {
        const words = sent.split(/\s+/).length;
        if (words > 30) {
          // Split at clause boundaries: semicolons, em-dashes, commas after 12+ words
          const clauses = sent.split(/(?<=[;—–])\s+|(?<=,)\s+(?=\w)/);
          let buffer = '';
          for (const clause of clauses) {
            const combined = buffer ? buffer + ' ' + clause : clause;
            if (combined.split(/\s+/).length > 22 && buffer) {
              broken.push(buffer.trim());
              buffer = clause;
            } else {
              buffer = combined;
            }
          }
          if (buffer.trim()) broken.push(buffer.trim());
        } else {
          broken.push(sent);
        }
      }
      sentences = broken;

      // Combine tiny fragments (<3 words) with the previous sentence
      const combined = [];
      for (const sent of sentences) {
        const words = sent.split(/\s+/).length;
        if (words < 3 && combined.length > 0) {
          combined[combined.length - 1] += ' ' + sent;
        } else {
          combined.push(sent);
        }
      }
      sentences = combined;

      // Build result with calculated pauses
      const result = [];
      for (let i = 0; i < sentences.length; i++) {
        const sent = sentences[i].trim();
        result.push(sent);

        if (i === sentences.length - 1) continue;

        const words = sent.split(/\s+/).length;
        const isDirective = DIRECTIVE_RX.test(sent);
        const hasEllipsis = ELLIPSIS_RX.test(sent);
        const isQuestion = sent.endsWith('?');

        let pause;
        if (isDirective && words <= 8) pause = 5;
        else if (isDirective) pause = 4;
        else if (hasEllipsis) pause = 3;
        else if (isQuestion) pause = 3;
        else if (words <= 5) pause = 2;
        else if (words >= 20) pause = 3;
        else pause = 2;

        result.push(`[PAUSE ${pause}]`);
      }

      return result.join(' ');
    });

    let fixed = processed.join('\n');
    fixed = fixed.replace(/(===\s*\w+\s*===)\s*(?!\[PAUSE)/gi, '$1\n[PAUSE 4]\n');
    return fixed;
  }

  /** Show/hide the fix timings button based on edit state */
  function updateFixTimingsVisibility() {
    showEl('fixTimingsBtn', _scriptEditedSinceGen);
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // SESSION HISTORY & STATS
  // ====================================================================
  async function renderSessionHistory() {
    const panel = $('sessionStatsPanel');
    const list = $('sessionHistoryList');
    if (!panel || !list) return;

    const history = (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [];
    if (history.length === 0) {
      panel.innerHTML = '';
      list.innerHTML = '<div class="library-empty">no sessions yet — complete a session to see stats</div>';
      return;
    }

    // Panel cleared — stats are shown in sidebarStats, sparkline appends here
    panel.innerHTML = '';

    // Recent sessions list (last 20)
    list.innerHTML = '';
    history.slice(0, 20).forEach((s, idx) => {
      const d = new Date(s.date);
      const dateStr = d.toLocaleDateString(undefined, { month: 'short', day: 'numeric' });
      const timeStr = d.toLocaleTimeString(undefined, { hour: 'numeric', minute: '2-digit' });
      const mins = Math.round((s.durationSec || 0) / 60);
      const hasScript = !!(s.script && s.script.length > 20);
      const status = s.completed ? `${mins}m` : `${mins}m · inc`;

      // Script preview — first ~150 chars, strip markers
      let preview = '';
      if (hasScript) {
        preview = s.script.replace(/===\s*\w+\s*===/gi, '').replace(/\[PAUSE\s+\d+\]/gi, '').trim();
        preview = preview.substring(0, 150).replace(/\s+/g, ' ');
        if (s.script.length > 150) preview += '…';
      }

      const item = document.createElement('div');
      item.className = 'history-item';
      item.innerHTML = `
        <div class="h-title">${dateStr} ${timeStr} · ${status}</div>
        <div class="h-meta">${escapeHtml(s.guide || '—')} · ${escapeHtml(s.method || '—')}${s.intentionText ? ' · ' + escapeHtml(s.intentionText.substring(0, 30)) : ''}</div>
        ${preview ? `<div class="h-preview">${escapeHtml(preview)}</div>` : '<div class="h-no-script">no script stored</div>'}
        <div class="h-actions">
          <button class="h-btn h-play" data-idx="${idx}" title="Replay session" ${hasScript ? '' : 'disabled'}>▶</button>
          <button class="h-btn h-edit" data-idx="${idx}" title="Edit script" ${hasScript ? '' : 'disabled'}>✎</button>
          <button class="h-btn h-delete" data-idx="${idx}" title="Delete">✕</button>
        </div>`;
      list.appendChild(item);
    });

    // Wire play buttons
    list.querySelectorAll('.h-play').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', async e => {
        const idx = parseInt(e.target.closest('.h-btn').dataset.idx, 10);
        const entry = history[idx];
        if (!entry?.script) { notify.warn('No script stored for this session.'); return; }
        replayFromHistory(entry);
      });
    });

    // Wire edit buttons — load script into editor without starting session
    list.querySelectorAll('.h-edit').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', async e => {
        const idx = parseInt(e.target.closest('.h-btn').dataset.idx, 10);
        const entry = history[idx];
        if (!entry?.script) { notify.warn('No script stored for this session.'); return; }
        editFromHistory(entry);
      });
    });

    // Wire delete buttons
    list.querySelectorAll('.h-delete').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', async e => {
        const idx = parseInt(e.target.closest('.h-btn').dataset.idx, 10);
        if (!confirm('Are you sure you want to delete this session?\n\nThis can\'t be undone.')) return;
        const h = (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [];
        h.splice(idx, 1);
        await idbSet('stillness_history_v1', h);
        await rebuildAnalytics(h);
        renderSessionHistory();
        renderSidebarStats();
        renderHeatmap();
        renderSparkline();
        notify.info('Session deleted.');
      });
    });
  }

  /** Replay a session from history — restores all settings and script */
  function replayFromHistory(entry) {
    // Restore settings
    if (entry.personaId) state.selectedPersonaId = entry.personaId;
    if (entry.methodId) state.selectedMethodId = entry.methodId;
    if (entry.intention) { state.intentionType = entry.intention; const el = $('intentionType'); if (el) el.value = entry.intention; }
    if (entry.length) { state.length = entry.length; const el = $('lengthSelect'); if (el) el.value = entry.length; }
    if (entry.soundscape) { state.soundscape = entry.soundscape; state.droneEnabled = entry.soundscape !== 'none'; const el = $('soundscapeSelect'); if (el) el.value = entry.soundscape; }
    if (entry.speechRate != null) { state.speechRate = entry.speechRate; const el = $('speechRate'); if (el) el.value = Math.round(entry.speechRate * 100); }
    if (entry.voicePitch != null) { state.voicePitch = entry.voicePitch; }
    if (entry.voiceVolume != null) { state.voiceVolume = entry.voiceVolume; }
    if (entry.droneVolume != null) { state.droneVolume = entry.droneVolume; }
    if (entry.vizOverride) { state.vizOverride = entry.vizOverride; const el = $('vizSelect'); if (el) el.value = entry.vizOverride; }
    if (entry.vizSettings) state.vizSettings = { ...state.vizSettings, ...entry.vizSettings };
    if (entry.duckingEnabled != null) { state.duckingEnabled = entry.duckingEnabled; const el = $('duckingToggle'); if (el) el.checked = entry.duckingEnabled; }
    if (entry.intentionText) { const el = $('intentionInput'); if (el) el.value = entry.intentionText; }
    if (entry.voiceName) state._savedVoiceName = entry.voiceName;

    // Load the script
    state.fullScript = entry.script;
    state.parsedScript = parseScript(entry.script);

    // Navigate to step 5 with the script loaded
    state.stepsCompleted = { 1: true, 2: true, 3: true, 4: true, 5: false };
    renderPersonaGrid(); renderPersonaDetail(); renderMethodGrid(); renderMethodDetail();
    updateIntentionHint();
    showScript();
    state.currentStep = 5;
    updateStepUI();
    switchScreen('setup-wizard');
    goToStep(5);
    // Close sidebar on mobile
    $('sidebar')?.classList.remove('open');
    $('sidebarOverlay')?.classList.remove('open');
    notify.success(`Session from ${new Date(entry.date).toLocaleDateString()} loaded — ready to replay.`);
  }

  /** Load a session from history into the script editor for editing */
  function editFromHistory(entry) {
    // Restore settings (same as replay)
    if (entry.personaId) state.selectedPersonaId = entry.personaId;
    if (entry.methodId) state.selectedMethodId = entry.methodId;
    if (entry.intention) { state.intentionType = entry.intention; const el = $('intentionType'); if (el) el.value = entry.intention; }
    if (entry.length) { state.length = entry.length; const el = $('lengthSelect'); if (el) el.value = entry.length; }
    if (entry.soundscape) { state.soundscape = entry.soundscape; state.droneEnabled = entry.soundscape !== 'none'; const el = $('soundscapeSelect'); if (el) el.value = entry.soundscape; }
    if (entry.intentionText) { const el = $('intentionInput'); if (el) el.value = entry.intentionText; }

    // Load script
    state.fullScript = entry.script;
    state.parsedScript = parseScript(entry.script);

    // Navigate to step 5 in edit mode
    state.stepsCompleted = { 1: true, 2: true, 3: true, 4: true, 5: false };
    renderPersonaGrid(); renderPersonaDetail(); renderMethodGrid(); renderMethodDetail();
    updateIntentionHint();
    showScript();
    showEl('generateScriptBtn', true);
    state.currentStep = 5;
    updateStepUI();
    switchScreen('setup-wizard');
    goToStep(5);
    $('sidebar')?.classList.remove('open');
    $('sidebarOverlay')?.classList.remove('open');
    // Focus the textarea for editing
    setTimeout(() => $('scriptText')?.focus(), 300);
    notify.info(`Script loaded for editing. Modify and press Begin when ready.`);
  }

  /** Populate sidebar stats and streak from session history */
  async function renderSidebarStats() {
    const statsEl = $('sidebarStats');
    const streakEl = $('sidebarStreak');
    const history = (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [];
    const analytics = await getAnalytics();

    // Use analytics for all-time aggregates (never decremented by deletions)
    const totalSessions = Math.max(analytics.comp.total, history.length);
    const totalMinutes = analytics.dur.n > 0
      ? Math.round(analytics.dur.sum / 60)
      : Math.round(history.reduce((sum, s) => sum + (s.durationSec || 0), 0) / 60);
    const completionPct = analytics.comp.total > 0
      ? Math.round(analytics.comp.finished / analytics.comp.total * 100)
      : (history.length > 0 ? Math.round(history.filter(s => s.completed).length / history.length * 100) : 0);

    if (totalSessions === 0) {
      if (statsEl) statsEl.innerHTML = '<div style="font-size:0.68rem;color:var(--text-faint);">No sessions yet</div>';
      if (streakEl) streakEl.textContent = 'New practitioner';
      return;
    }

    // Streak calculated from history dates (temporal — reflects current record)
    const today = new Date(); today.setHours(0,0,0,0);
    const dayMs = 86400000;
    const sessionDays = [...new Set(history.map(s => { const d = new Date(s.date); d.setHours(0,0,0,0); return d.getTime(); }))].sort((a,b) => b - a);
    let streak = 0, freezesUsed = 0, checkDay = today.getTime();
    for (const day of sessionDays) {
      const gap = (checkDay - day) / dayMs;
      if (gap <= 1) { streak++; checkDay = day; }
      else if (gap === 2 && freezesUsed < 2) { streak++; freezesUsed++; checkDay = day; }
      else break;
    }
    if (streakEl) streakEl.textContent = streak > 0 ? `${streak}-day streak` : `${totalSessions} sessions`;

    if (statsEl) {
      let html = `
        <div class="sidebar-stat-row"><span>Sessions</span><span class="sidebar-stat-val">${totalSessions}</span></div>
        <div class="sidebar-stat-row"><span>Minutes</span><span class="sidebar-stat-val">${totalMinutes}</span></div>
        <div class="sidebar-stat-row"><span>Streak</span><span class="sidebar-stat-val">${streak} days</span></div>
        <div class="sidebar-stat-row"><span>Completion</span><span class="sidebar-stat-val">${completionPct}%</span></div>`;

      // Analytics insights (after 2+ tracked sessions)
      if (analytics.comp.total >= 2) {
        try {
          const ins = deriveInsights(analytics);
          const hourLabel = ins.peakHour < 12 ? `${ins.peakHour || 12}am` : `${ins.peakHour === 12 ? 12 : ins.peakHour - 12}pm`;
          html += `<div style="margin-top:6px;border-top:1px solid var(--glass-border);padding-top:6px;">`;
          if (ins.avgImprovement && parseFloat(ins.avgImprovement) > 0) {
            html += `<div class="sidebar-stat-row"><span>Avg improvement</span><span class="sidebar-stat-val" style="color:var(--accent-green);">+${ins.avgImprovement}</span></div>`;
          }
          html += `<div class="sidebar-stat-row"><span>Peak time</span><span class="sidebar-stat-val">${hourLabel}</span></div>`;
          if (ins.favPersona) html += `<div class="sidebar-stat-row"><span>Fav guide</span><span class="sidebar-stat-val" style="font-size:0.7rem;">${ins.favPersona}</span></div>`;
          if (ins.favSoundscape && ins.favSoundscape !== 'none') html += `<div class="sidebar-stat-row"><span>Fav sound</span><span class="sidebar-stat-val" style="font-size:0.7rem;">${ins.favSoundscape}</span></div>`;
          html += `</div>`;
        } catch {}
      }

      statsEl.innerHTML = html;
    }
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // STATS CHARTS MODAL — Canvas 2D chart rendering
  // ====================================================================
  const CHART_COLORS = {
    cyan: '#00e5ff', amber: '#ffab00', magenta: '#ff4081', purple: '#ba68c8',
    green: '#39ff8e', blue: '#4fc3f7', orange: '#ff9800', teal: '#26a69a',
    bars: ['#4fc3f7','#00e5ff','#26a69a','#39ff8e','#ffab00','#ff9800','#ff4081','#ba68c8','#7c4dff','#e0e0e0'],
    gridLine: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.08)', label: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.5)', title: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.7)',
  };

  function drawBarChart(canvasId, labels, values, color) {
    const canvas = $(canvasId); if (!canvas) return;
    const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
    const W = canvas.offsetWidth || 360, H = canvas.offsetHeight || 200;
    canvas.width = W * dpr; canvas.height = H * dpr;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d'); ctx.scale(dpr, dpr);
    if (!values.length || values.every(v => v === 0)) { ctx.fillStyle = CHART_COLORS.label; ctx.font = '12px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'center'; ctx.fillText('No data yet', W/2, H/2); return; }
    const pad = { top: 10, right: 10, bottom: 40, left: 32 };
    const chartW = W - pad.left - pad.right, chartH = H - pad.top - pad.bottom;
    const maxVal = Math.max(...values, 1);
    const barW = Math.min(40, (chartW / labels.length) * 0.65);
    const gap = chartW / labels.length;
    // Grid lines
    ctx.strokeStyle = CHART_COLORS.gridLine; ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;
    for (let i = 0; i <= 4; i++) { const y = pad.top + chartH * (1 - i/4); ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(pad.left, y); ctx.lineTo(W - pad.right, y); ctx.stroke(); }
    // Bars
    labels.forEach((label, i) => {
      const barH = (values[i] / maxVal) * chartH;
      const x = pad.left + gap * i + (gap - barW) / 2;
      const y = pad.top + chartH - barH;
      const c = Array.isArray(color) ? color[i % color.length] : color;
      ctx.fillStyle = c; ctx.beginPath();
      const r = Math.min(3, barW/2);
      ctx.moveTo(x, y + r); ctx.arcTo(x, y, x + r, y, r); ctx.arcTo(x + barW, y, x + barW, y + r, r);
      ctx.lineTo(x + barW, pad.top + chartH); ctx.lineTo(x, pad.top + chartH); ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();
      // Value label
      ctx.fillStyle = CHART_COLORS.title; ctx.font = 'bold 10px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'center';
      ctx.fillText(values[i], x + barW/2, y - 4);
      // Axis label
      ctx.fillStyle = CHART_COLORS.label; ctx.font = '9px sans-serif';
      ctx.save(); ctx.translate(x + barW/2, pad.top + chartH + 6);
      if (labels.length > 6) { ctx.rotate(-0.5); ctx.textAlign = 'right'; } else { ctx.textAlign = 'center'; }
      ctx.fillText(label.length > 12 ? label.slice(0,11) + '…' : label, 0, 8); ctx.restore();
    });
  }

  function drawLineChart(canvasId, labels, values, color) {
    const canvas = $(canvasId); if (!canvas) return;
    const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
    const W = canvas.offsetWidth || 740, H = canvas.offsetHeight || 220;
    canvas.width = W * dpr; canvas.height = H * dpr;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d'); ctx.scale(dpr, dpr);
    if (!values.length) return;
    const pad = { top: 14, right: 14, bottom: 36, left: 32 };
    const chartW = W - pad.left - pad.right, chartH = H - pad.top - pad.bottom;
    const maxVal = Math.max(...values, 1);
    const xStep = chartW / (labels.length - 1 || 1);
    // Grid
    ctx.strokeStyle = CHART_COLORS.gridLine; ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;
    for (let i = 0; i <= 4; i++) { const y = pad.top + chartH * (1 - i/4); ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(pad.left, y); ctx.lineTo(W - pad.right, y); ctx.stroke(); }
    // Fill area
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(pad.left, pad.top + chartH);
    values.forEach((v, i) => { ctx.lineTo(pad.left + i * xStep, pad.top + chartH - (v / maxVal) * chartH); });
    ctx.lineTo(pad.left + (values.length-1) * xStep, pad.top + chartH); ctx.closePath();
    ctx.fillStyle = color.replace(')', ',0.12)').replace('rgb', 'rgba'); ctx.fill();
    // Line
    ctx.beginPath();
    values.forEach((v, i) => { const x = pad.left + i * xStep, y = pad.top + chartH - (v / maxVal) * chartH; i === 0 ? ctx.moveTo(x, y) : ctx.lineTo(x, y); });
    ctx.strokeStyle = color; ctx.lineWidth = 2; ctx.stroke();
    // Dots
    values.forEach((v, i) => { const x = pad.left + i * xStep, y = pad.top + chartH - (v / maxVal) * chartH; ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x, y, 3, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fillStyle = color; ctx.fill(); });
    // Peak annotation
    const peakIdx = values.indexOf(Math.max(...values));
    if (values[peakIdx] > 0) {
      const px = pad.left + peakIdx * xStep, py = pad.top + chartH - (values[peakIdx] / maxVal) * chartH;
      ctx.fillStyle = CHART_COLORS.amber; ctx.font = 'bold 10px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'center';
      ctx.fillText(`Peak: ${labels[peakIdx]} (${values[peakIdx]})`, Math.min(Math.max(px, 60), W - 60), py - 10);
    }
    // X labels
    ctx.fillStyle = CHART_COLORS.label; ctx.font = '9px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'center';
    labels.forEach((l, i) => { if (labels.length <= 10 || i % 2 === 0) ctx.fillText(l, pad.left + i * xStep, H - pad.bottom + 16); });
  }

  function drawDonutChart(canvasId, segments) {
    const canvas = $(canvasId); if (!canvas) return;
    const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
    const W = canvas.offsetWidth || 360, H = canvas.offsetHeight || 220;
    canvas.width = W * dpr; canvas.height = H * dpr;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d'); ctx.scale(dpr, dpr);
    const total = segments.reduce((s, seg) => s + seg.value, 0);
    if (total === 0) { ctx.fillStyle = CHART_COLORS.label; ctx.font = '12px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'center'; ctx.fillText('No data yet', W/2, H/2); return; }
    const cx = W / 2, cy = H / 2 - 6, outerR = Math.min(W, H) / 2 - 30, innerR = outerR * 0.55;
    let angle = -Math.PI / 2;
    segments.forEach(seg => {
      const sweep = (seg.value / total) * Math.PI * 2;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx, cy, outerR, angle, angle + sweep); ctx.arc(cx, cy, innerR, angle + sweep, angle, true); ctx.closePath();
      ctx.fillStyle = seg.color; ctx.fill();
      // Label
      const mid = angle + sweep / 2;
      const lx = cx + Math.cos(mid) * (outerR + 16), ly = cy + Math.sin(mid) * (outerR + 16);
      ctx.fillStyle = CHART_COLORS.title; ctx.font = '10px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = Math.cos(mid) > 0 ? 'left' : 'right';
      ctx.fillText(`${seg.label} ${Math.round(seg.value / total * 100)}%`, lx, ly);
      angle += sweep;
    });
  }

  function drawHorizBars(canvasId, labels, values, maxVal, colors) {
    const canvas = $(canvasId); if (!canvas) return;
    const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
    const W = canvas.offsetWidth || 360, H = canvas.offsetHeight || 200;
    canvas.width = W * dpr; canvas.height = H * dpr;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d'); ctx.scale(dpr, dpr);
    const pad = { left: 80, right: 40, top: 10, bottom: 10 };
    const rowH = (H - pad.top - pad.bottom) / labels.length;
    const barMaxW = W - pad.left - pad.right;
    labels.forEach((label, i) => {
      const y = pad.top + i * rowH;
      const barW = (values[i] / (maxVal || 1)) * barMaxW;
      ctx.fillStyle = colors[i % colors.length]; ctx.beginPath();
      const r = 3; ctx.moveTo(pad.left, y + 4); ctx.lineTo(pad.left + barW - r, y + 4); ctx.arcTo(pad.left + barW, y + 4, pad.left + barW, y + rowH - 8, r); ctx.arcTo(pad.left + barW, y + rowH - 8, pad.left + barW - r, y + rowH - 8, r); ctx.lineTo(pad.left, y + rowH - 8); ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();
      ctx.fillStyle = CHART_COLORS.label; ctx.font = '10px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'right';
      ctx.fillText(label, pad.left - 6, y + rowH/2 + 3);
      ctx.fillStyle = CHART_COLORS.title; ctx.font = 'bold 10px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'left';
      ctx.fillText(values[i].toFixed(2), pad.left + barW + 6, y + rowH/2 + 3);
    });
  }

  function drawFeatureGrid(canvasId, featBitmask) {
    const canvas = $(canvasId); if (!canvas) return;
    const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
    const W = canvas.offsetWidth || 360, H = canvas.offsetHeight || 200;
    canvas.width = W * dpr; canvas.height = H * dpr;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d'); ctx.scale(dpr, dpr);
    const features = [
      { name: 'Affirmations', bit: 1 }, { name: 'Programs', bit: 2 }, { name: 'Custom Persona', bit: 4 },
      { name: 'Skip-to-Script', bit: 8 }, { name: 'Timing Fix', bit: 16 }, { name: 'Share', bit: 32 },
      { name: 'Backup', bit: 64 }, { name: 'Double Induction', bit: 128 },
    ];
    const rowH = (H - 10) / features.length;
    features.forEach((f, i) => {
      const y = 8 + i * rowH;
      const used = !!(featBitmask & f.bit);
      ctx.fillStyle = used ? CHART_COLORS.cyan : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.06)';
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.roundRect(20, y, W - 40, rowH - 4, 4); ctx.fill();
      ctx.fillStyle = used ? '#111' : CHART_COLORS.label; ctx.font = `${used ? 'bold ' : ''}11px sans-serif`; ctx.textAlign = 'left';
      ctx.fillText(`${used ? '✓' : '○'}  ${f.name}`, 30, y + rowH/2 + 1);
    });
  }

  // Chart render dispatch — maps tile data-chart to render calls
  let _statsAnalytics = null;
  function renderChart(tile) {
    const chart = tile.dataset.chart;
    const a = _statsAnalytics; if (!a) return;
    const sorted = (map) => Object.entries(map || {}).sort((x,y) => y[1] - x[1]);
    const topItems = (map, n) => { const s = sorted(map); return { labels: s.slice(0,n).map(e => e[0]), values: s.slice(0,n).map(e => e[1]) }; };
    switch(chart) {
      case 'persona': { const d = topItems(a.p, 8); drawBarChart('chartPersona', d.labels, d.values, CHART_COLORS.bars); break; }
      case 'method': { const d = topItems(a.m, 8); drawBarChart('chartMethod', d.labels, d.values, CHART_COLORS.bars); break; }
      case 'intention': { const d = topItems(a.i, 8); drawBarChart('chartIntention', d.labels, d.values, CHART_COLORS.bars); break; }
      case 'soundscape': { const d = topItems(a.s, 8); drawBarChart('chartSoundscape', d.labels, d.values, CHART_COLORS.bars); break; }
      case 'hourly': { drawLineChart('chartHourly', Array.from({length:24}, (_,i) => i.toString()), a.hr, CHART_COLORS.cyan); break; }
      case 'weekday': { drawBarChart('chartWeekday', ['Sun','Mon','Tue','Wed','Thu','Fri','Sat'], a.dw, CHART_COLORS.bars); break; }
      case 'mood': {
        if (a.mood.n > 0) {
          const avgPre = a.mood.preSum / a.mood.n, avgPost = a.mood.postSum > 0 ? a.mood.postSum / a.mood.n : null;
          const mL = avgPost ? ['Pre','Post'] : ['Pre'], mV = avgPost ? [+avgPre.toFixed(1), +avgPost.toFixed(1)] : [+avgPre.toFixed(1)];
          drawBarChart('chartMood', mL, mV, [CHART_COLORS.blue, CHART_COLORS.green]);
        } else drawBarChart('chartMood', [], [], CHART_COLORS.cyan);
        break;
      }
      case 'completion': {
        const other = a.comp.total - a.comp.finished - a.comp.emergency;
        drawDonutChart('chartCompletion', [
          { label: 'Finished', value: a.comp.finished, color: CHART_COLORS.cyan },
          { label: 'Emergency', value: a.comp.emergency, color: CHART_COLORS.amber },
          { label: 'Incomplete', value: Math.max(0, other), color: CHART_COLORS.green },
        ]); break;
      }
      case 'settings': {
        if (a.cfg.n > 0) {
          const cL = ['Rate','Pitch','Narr Vol','Drone'];
          const cV = [a.cfg.rateSum/a.cfg.n, a.cfg.pitchSum/a.cfg.n, a.cfg.volSum/a.cfg.n, a.cfg.droneSum/a.cfg.n];
          drawHorizBars('chartSettings', cL, cV, 1.2, [CHART_COLORS.cyan, CHART_COLORS.blue, CHART_COLORS.amber, CHART_COLORS.green]);
        } else drawBarChart('chartSettings', [], [], CHART_COLORS.cyan);
        break;
      }
      case 'features': drawFeatureGrid('chartFeatures', a.feat); break;
    }
  }

  function renderAllCharts() {
    document.querySelectorAll('.stats-tile').forEach(tile => renderChart(tile));
  }

  async function openStatsModal() {
    const a = await getAnalytics();
    _statsAnalytics = a;
    const modal = $('statsModal');
    if (a.comp.total < 1) {
      $('statsKpiGrid').innerHTML = '';
      $('statsGrid').style.display = 'none';
      $('statsEmptyMsg').style.display = '';
      modal.style.display = 'flex'; return;
    }
    $('statsEmptyMsg').style.display = 'none';
    $('statsGrid').style.display = '';
    const ins = deriveInsights(a);
    const durMin = Math.floor(ins.avgDurationSec / 60), durSec = ins.avgDurationSec % 60;
    const hrLbl = ins.peakHour < 12 ? `${ins.peakHour || 12}am` : `${ins.peakHour === 12 ? 12 : ins.peakHour - 12}pm`;
    $('statsKpiGrid').innerHTML = [
      { val: ins.totalSessions, label: 'sessions' },
      { val: `${ins.completionRate}%`, label: 'completed' },
      { val: ins.avgImprovement && parseFloat(ins.avgImprovement) > 0 ? `+${ins.avgImprovement}` : (ins.avgImprovement || '—'), label: 'mood gain' },
      { val: `${durMin}m${durSec ? durSec + 's' : ''}`, label: 'avg duration' },
      { val: hrLbl, label: 'peak hour' },
      { val: ins.peakDayName.slice(0,3), label: 'peak day' },
    ].map(k => `<div class="stats-kpi"><div class="stats-kpi-val">${k.val}</div><div class="stats-kpi-label">${k.label}</div></div>`).join('');

    modal.style.display = 'flex';
    // Render after display so canvas has layout dimensions
    requestAnimationFrame(() => renderAllCharts());
  }

  function closeStatsModal() { $('statsModal').style.display = 'none'; _statsAnalytics = null; }

  function toggleStatsTile(tile) {
    const wasExpanded = tile.classList.contains('expanded');
    // Collapse all first
    document.querySelectorAll('.stats-tile.expanded').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('expanded'));
    if (!wasExpanded) tile.classList.add('expanded');
    // Re-render affected charts after CSS transition
    setTimeout(() => {
      if (wasExpanded) renderChart(tile);
      else document.querySelectorAll('.stats-tile').forEach(t => renderChart(t));
    }, 280);
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // EXPORT, SHARE, BACKUP/RESTORE
  // ====================================================================
  function exportScript() {
    const script = $('scriptText')?.value?.trim();
    if (!script) { notify.warn('No script to export.'); return; }
    const persona = getPersona(), method = getMethod();
    const header = `# Hypnosis Script\n# Guide: ${persona.name} | Method: ${method.name} | Length: ${state.length}\n# Generated: ${new Date().toLocaleDateString()}\n\n`;
    const blob = new Blob([header + script], { type: 'text/plain' });
    const a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    a.download = `hypnosis-${method.id}-${state.length}-${Date.now()}.txt`;
    a.click(); URL.revokeObjectURL(a.href);
    notify.success('Script downloaded.');
  }

  async function shareConfig() {
    markFeatureUsed(FEAT.SHARE);
    // Compact URI-safe params — no gzip overhead for small payloads
    const params = new URLSearchParams();
    params.set('p', state.selectedPersonaId);
    params.set('m', state.selectedMethodId);
    params.set('i', state.intentionType);
    params.set('l', state.length);
    params.set('s', state.soundscape);
    params.set('r', String(Math.round(state.speechRate * 100)));
    params.set('v', state.vizOverride || 'auto');
    const intentText = $('intentionInput')?.value?.trim();
    if (intentText) params.set('t', intentText.slice(0, 200));
    const aff = $('userAffirmations')?.value?.trim();
    if (aff) params.set('a', aff.slice(0, 300));

    const url = window.location.href.split('#')[0].split('?')[0] + '#cfg=' + params.toString();
    if (navigator.share && navigator.canShare?.({ url })) {
      try { await navigator.share({ title: 'Hypnosis Session Config', text: `Try this ${getMethod().name} session with ${getPersona().name}`, url }); return; } catch(e) {}
    }
    try { await navigator.clipboard.writeText(url); notify.success('Share link copied to clipboard.'); }
    catch(e) { prompt('Copy this share link:', url); }
  }

  async function loadSharedConfig() {
    const hash = window.location.hash;
    if (!hash.startsWith('#cfg=')) return;
    const paramStr = hash.slice(5);
    try {
      const params = new URLSearchParams(paramStr);
      const personaId = params.get('p');
      const methodId = params.get('m');
      const intentType = params.get('i');
      const length = params.get('l');
      const soundscape = params.get('s');
      const rate = params.get('r');
      const viz = params.get('v');
      const intentText = params.get('t');
      const aff = params.get('a');

      // Apply settings
      if (personaId && state.personas.find(p => p.id === personaId)) state.selectedPersonaId = personaId;
      if (methodId && METHODS.find(m => m.id === methodId)) state.selectedMethodId = methodId;
      if (intentType && INTENTION_TYPES[intentType]) { state.intentionType = intentType; $('intentionType').value = intentType; }
      if (length && PHASE_DURATIONS[length]) { state.length = length; $('lengthSelect').value = length; }
      if (soundscape) { state.soundscape = soundscape; state.droneEnabled = soundscape !== 'none'; const el = $('soundscapeSelect'); if (el) el.value = soundscape; }
      if (rate) state.speechRate = Math.max(0.5, Math.min(1, parseInt(rate, 10) / 100));
      if (viz) { state.vizOverride = viz; const el = $('vizSelect'); if (el) el.value = viz; }
      if (intentText) { const el = $('intentionInput'); if (el) el.value = decodeURIComponent(intentText).slice(0, 500); }
      if (aff) { const el = $('userAffirmations'); if (el) el.value = decodeURIComponent(aff).slice(0, 500); }

      renderPersonaGrid(); renderPersonaDetail(); renderMethodGrid(); renderMethodDetail();
      updateIntentionHint(); updateStepUI();

      // Onboarding banner for the recipient
      const persona = getPersona();
      const method = getMethod();
      notify.info(`Shared config loaded: ${persona.name} · ${method.name} · ${length || 'medium'}. Review settings and generate when ready.`, 8000);

      // Mark steps as complete so they can jump to generate
      state.stepsCompleted = { 1: true, 2: true, 3: true, 4: true, 5: false };
      goToStep(4); // Start at Configure so they can review

      // Clean URL
      history.replaceState(null, '', window.location.pathname + window.location.search);
    } catch(e) {
      // Fallback: try old gzip+base64 format for backward compat
      try {
        const bytes = Uint8Array.from(atob(paramStr), c => c.charCodeAt(0));
        const stream = new Blob([bytes]).stream().pipeThrough(new DecompressionStream('gzip'));
        const json = await new Response(stream).text();
        const cfg = JSON.parse(json);
        if (cfg.p) state.selectedPersonaId = cfg.p;
        if (cfg.m) state.selectedMethodId = cfg.m;
        if (cfg.i) { state.intentionType = cfg.i; $('intentionType').value = cfg.i; }
        if (cfg.l) { state.length = cfg.l; $('lengthSelect').value = cfg.l; }
        renderPersonaGrid(); renderPersonaDetail(); renderMethodGrid(); renderMethodDetail(); updateStepUI();
        notify.info('Shared config loaded (legacy format). Review and generate.');
        history.replaceState(null, '', window.location.pathname + window.location.search);
      } catch(e2) { console.error('Failed to parse shared config:', e2); }
    }
  }

  async function exportBackup() {
    markFeatureUsed(FEAT.BACKUP);
    const backup = { version: 3, exportedAt: Date.now(), personas: loadCustomPersonas(), history: (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [], program: (await idbGet('stillness_program_v1')) || null, profile: getProfile(), analytics: (await idbGet(ANALYTICS_KEY)) || null };
    const json = JSON.stringify(backup);
    let blob;
    try {
      const stream = new Blob([json]).stream().pipeThrough(new CompressionStream('gzip'));
      blob = await new Response(stream).blob();
    } catch(e) { blob = new Blob([json], { type: 'application/json' }); }
    const a = document.createElement('a'); a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    a.download = `stillness-backup-${new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10)}.gz`;
    a.click(); URL.revokeObjectURL(a.href); notify.success('Backup exported (.gz).');
  }

  async function importBackup(file) {
    try {
      let text;
      try {
        const stream = file.stream().pipeThrough(new DecompressionStream('gzip'));
        text = await new Response(stream).text();
      } catch(e) {
        text = await file.text();
      }
      const backup = JSON.parse(text);
      if (!backup.version) { notify.error('Invalid backup file.'); return; }
      const ep = loadCustomPersonas(), eIds = new Set(ep.map(p => p.id));
      const np = (backup.personas||[]).filter(p => !eIds.has(p.id));
      if (np.length) { saveCustomPersonas([...ep,...np]); refreshPersonas(); renderPersonaGrid(); }
      const eh = (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1'))||[], ehIds = new Set(eh.map(h => h.id));
      const nh = (backup.history||[]).filter(h => !ehIds.has(h.id));
      if (nh.length) { const m = [...nh,...eh].sort((a,b)=>(b.date||0)-(a.date||0)); m.length = Math.min(m.length,50); await idbSet('stillness_history_v1',m); renderSessionHistory(); }
      if (backup.program && !(await idbGet('stillness_program_v1'))) { await idbSet('stillness_program_v1', backup.program); renderPrograms(); }
      if (backup.analytics && !(await idbGet(ANALYTICS_KEY))) { await idbSet(ANALYTICS_KEY, backup.analytics); }
      // Restore profile if present and no existing profile
      if (backup.profile && !$('pfName')?.value?.trim()) {
        const p = backup.profile;
        if (p.name) { const el = $('pfName'); if (el) el.value = p.name; }
        if (p.pronouns) { const el = $('pfPronouns'); if (el) el.value = p.pronouns; }
        if (p.age) { const el = $('pfAge'); if (el) el.value = p.age; }
        if (p.experience) { const el = $('pfExperience'); if (el) el.value = p.experience; }
        if (p.about) { const el = $('pfAbout'); if (el) el.value = p.about; }
        if (p.appearance) { const el = $('pfAppearance'); if (el) el.value = p.appearance; }
        if (p.goals) { const el = $('pfGoals'); if (el) el.value = p.goals; }
        saveProfile();
      }
      notify.success(`Imported: ${np.length} personas, ${nh.length} sessions.`);
    } catch(e) { notify.error('Import failed: ' + e.message); }
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // TRANSCRIPT
  // ====================================================================
  function populateTranscript() {
    const panel = $('transcriptPanel');
    if (!panel || !state.parsedScript) return;
    const phases = ['settling','induction','deepener','work','emergence'];
    const labels = { settling:'Settling', induction:'Induction', deepener:'Deepener', work:'Work', emergence:'Emergence' };
    let html = '';
    for (const phase of phases) {
      const text = state.parsedScript[phase];
      if (!text || text.trim().length < 10) continue;
      const clean = text.replace(/^===\s*\w+\s*===\s*/i, '').replace(/\[PAUSE\s+\d+\]/gi, ' ⋯ ').trim();
      html += `<div class="t-phase">${labels[phase]}</div><div>${escapeHtml(clean)}</div>`;
    }
    panel.innerHTML = html;
  }

  function toggleTranscript() {
    const panel = $('transcriptPanel');
    if (!panel) return;
    panel.classList.toggle('visible');
    const btn = $('transcriptToggle');
    if (btn) btn.textContent = panel.classList.contains('visible') ? '✕ close' : '📜 script';
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // SESSION PLAYER
  // ====================================================================
  async function startSession() {
    // Emergency cooldown check
    if (state._cooldownUntil && Date.now() < state._cooldownUntil) {
      const remaining = Math.ceil((state._cooldownUntil - Date.now()) / 1000);
      notify.warn(`Please wait ${remaining}s before starting another session.`);
      return;
    }

    const scriptText = $('scriptText').value.trim();
    if (!scriptText) { notify.warn('Generate or paste a script first.'); return; }

    // If script was edited, offer to fix pause timings
    if (_scriptEditedSinceGen) {
      const fix = confirm('You\'ve edited the script. Would you like to recalculate pause timings to match your changes?\n\n• Yes = auto-fix [PAUSE] markers based on sentence length\n• No = keep current timings as-is');
      if (fix) {
        const fixed = fixScriptTimings(scriptText);
        $('scriptText').value = fixed;
        state.fullScript = fixed;
        state.parsedScript = parseScript(fixed);
        showScript();
        notify.success('Pause timings recalculated.');
      }
      _scriptEditedSinceGen = false;
      updateFixTimingsVisibility();
    }

    // Daily session cap
    if (!(await checkDailyCap())) return;

    // Check TTS availability
    const voiceList = (typeof speechSynthesis !== 'undefined') ? speechSynthesis.getVoices() : [];
    if (voiceList.length === 0) {
      if (!confirm('No text-to-speech voices are available in this browser. The session will run silently (visuals only). Continue anyway?')) return;
    }

    // Stop any configure-tab previews before starting session
    if (typeof _stopAllPreviews === 'function') _stopAllPreviews();

    state.fullScript = scriptText;
    state.parsedScript = parseScript(scriptText);
    state.voice = getSelectedVoice();
    state.abortFlag = false;
    state._finishing = false;
    state._sessionStartTime = Date.now();
    state._currentPhase = 'settling';
    const method = getMethod();

    // Double induction: pick a contrasting second voice
    state._doubleInduction = method.id === 'double-induction';
    state._secondVoice = null;
    if (state._doubleInduction) {
      const voices = speechSynthesis.getVoices().filter(v => v.lang.startsWith('en') && v.name !== state.voice?.name);
      // Try to find an opposite-gender voice for maximum contrast
      const primaryName = (state.voice?.name || '').toLowerCase();
      const isMale = /male|daniel|james|david|mark|george/i.test(primaryName) && !/female/i.test(primaryName);
      const opposite = voices.find(v => isMale ? /female|samantha|karen|moira|zira/i.test(v.name) : /male|daniel|james|david|mark/i.test(v.name) && !/female/i.test(v.name));
      state._secondVoice = opposite || voices[0] || null;
      if (state._secondVoice) {
        notify.info(`Double induction: ${state.voice?.name || 'primary'} + ${state._secondVoice.name}`);
      }
    }

    switchScreen('session-screen');
    document.body.classList.add('in-session');
    $('personaIndicator').textContent = '· ' + getPersona().name.toLowerCase() + ' ·';
    $('methodIndicator').textContent = '· ' + method.name.toLowerCase() + ' ·';

    // Reset progress UI
    $('sessionProgressFill').style.width = '0%';
    updatePhaseDots(-1);

    // Apply HUD visibility toggles from Configure tab
    const h = state.hud;
    const $s = (id, vis) => { const el = $(id); if (el) el.style.display = vis ? '' : 'none'; };
    $s('fixationDot', h.fixationDot);
    $s('textDisplay', h.textDisplay);
    $s('phaseDots', h.phaseDots);
    $s('phaseIndicator', h.phaseLabel);
    document.querySelector('.session-progress-wrap')?.style.setProperty('display', h.progressBar ? '' : 'none');
    $s('sessionTime', h.sessionTime);
    $s('personaIndicator', h.labels);
    $s('methodIndicator', h.labels);
    $s('audioIndicator', h.labels);

    // Apply visual override (user selection or method default)
    const vizChoice = state.vizOverride === 'auto' ? method.visual : state.vizOverride;
    if (vizChoice === 'none') {
      // Black screen only — skip visual setup
      const stage = $('stage');
      Array.from(stage.children).forEach(c => {
        if (!c.classList.contains('fixation-dot') && !c.classList.contains('audio-indicator')
          && !c.classList.contains('persona-indicator') && !c.classList.contains('method-indicator')
          && !c.classList.contains('session-progress-wrap') && !c.classList.contains('transcript-panel')) c.remove();
      });
    } else {
      setupVisual(vizChoice);
    }
    populateTranscript();
    $('transcriptPanel')?.classList.remove('visible');
    const tBtn = $('transcriptToggle');
    if (tBtn) tBtn.textContent = '📜 script';

    // Start soundscape (replaces old drone toggle)
    if (state.soundscape && state.soundscape !== 'none') {
      try {
        await drone.start(state.droneVolume, state.soundscape);
        $('audioIndicator').textContent = '· ' + state.soundscape + ' ·';
      } catch(e) {
        notify.info('Audio unavailable — tap the screen to enable audio, then try again.');
      }
    }

    // Haptic marker — double-pulse on session start (Android/Chrome)
    vibrateSessionMarker();

    // Warm overlay for sleep sessions (blue-light reduction)
    setSleepOverlay(state.intentionType === 'sleep');

    // Media Session API — lock-screen controls for mobile
    setMediaSession(true);

    // Reset post-session controls for fresh state
    const postSlider = $('postStateSlider'); if (postSlider) { postSlider.value = 5; }
    const postVal = $('postStateVal'); if (postVal) postVal.textContent = '5';
    const alertSlider = $('alertnessSlider'); if (alertSlider) { alertSlider.value = 7; }
    const alertVal = $('alertnessVal'); if (alertVal) alertVal.textContent = '7';
    const journal = $('journalText'); if (journal) journal.value = '';

    // Wake Lock — prevent screen timeout during session
    try {
      if (navigator.wakeLock) {
        state._wakeLock = await navigator.wakeLock.request('screen');
        state._wakeLock.addEventListener('release', () => { state._wakeLock = null; });
      }
    } catch(e) { /* Wake Lock not available or denied */ }

    // Content warning for advanced/intense methods
    const needsWarning = method.category === 'advanced' || ['drill-instructor','dominatrix','interrogator','commander'].includes(getPersona().id);
    if (needsWarning) {
      const warningShown = await new Promise(resolve => {
        const proceed = confirm(
          'This session uses advanced techniques that may produce intense experiences including dissociation, hallucination, or strong emotional responses.\n\n' +
          'Ensure you are in a safe, comfortable environment. Do not drive or operate machinery after.\n\n' +
          'The "end & re-alert" button is always available.\n\nProceed?'
        );
        resolve(proceed);
      });
      if (!warningShown) {
        switchScreen('setup-wizard');
        document.body.classList.remove('in-session');
        await drone.stop(); stopVisuals();
        try { state._wakeLock?.release(); } catch(e) {}
        return;
      }
    }

    // Session time tracker
    state._timeInterval = setInterval(() => {
      if (state.paused) return;
      const elapsed = Math.round((Date.now() - state._sessionStartTime) / 1000);
      const mins = Math.floor(elapsed / 60);
      const secs = elapsed % 60;
      const timeEl = $('sessionTime');
      if (timeEl) timeEl.textContent = `${mins}:${String(secs).padStart(2,'0')} elapsed`;
    }, 1000);

    const phases = ['settling','induction','deepener','work','emergence'];
    const phaseLabels = { settling: 'settling', induction: 'going inward', deepener: 'deeper', work: method.category === 'demonstration' ? 'the effect' : 'transformation', emergence: 're-alerting' };

    // Safety timeout — absolute max session duration (expected × 2 + 5 min buffer)
    const durations = PHASE_DURATIONS[state.length] || PHASE_DURATIONS.medium;
    const expectedSec = Object.values(durations).reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
    state._safetyTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
      if (!state._finishing && state._sessionStartTime) {
        notify.warn('Session exceeded maximum expected duration — auto-finishing.');
        state._finishing = true;
        state.abortFlag = true;
        speechSynthesis.cancel();
        finishSession(false);
      }
    }, (expectedSec * 2 + 300) * 1000);

    for (let pi = 0; pi < phases.length; pi++) {
      const phase = phases[pi];
      if (state.abortFlag) break;
      const phaseText = state.parsedScript[phase];
      if (!phaseText || phaseText.trim().length < 10) continue;

      // Update phase state
      state._currentPhase = phase;
      $('phaseIndicator').textContent = phaseLabels[phase];

      // Update phase dots
      updatePhaseDots(pi);

      // Update progress bar
      const pct = Math.round((pi / phases.length) * 100);
      $('sessionProgressFill').style.width = pct + '%';

      // Modulate drone frequency per phase
      if (state.droneEnabled && drone.running) drone.setPhaseFreq(phase);

      const cleanText = phaseText.replace(/^===\s*\w+\s*===\s*/i, '').trim();
      await speakScript(cleanText);
    }

    // Complete progress bar
    $('sessionProgressFill').style.width = '100%';
    updatePhaseDots(5);

    // Always finish the session — if abortFlag was set by emergencyEnd,
    // that path calls finishSession(true) itself, so only call if not aborting.
    // Guard against double-finish with a flag.
    if (!state.abortFlag && !state._finishing) {
      state._finishing = true;
      finishSession(false);
    }
  }

  // Interruptible sleep — checks abortFlag & paused state in 200ms chunks so
  // pause/end during a [PAUSE n] marker responds quickly instead of waiting
  // for the whole sleep to finish.
  async function interruptibleSleep(totalMs, bypassAbort = false) {
    const CHUNK = 200;
    let elapsed = 0;
    while (elapsed < totalMs) {
      if (!bypassAbort && state.abortFlag) return;
      while (state.paused && !state.abortFlag) { await sleep(CHUNK); }
      const remaining = totalMs - elapsed;
      await sleep(Math.min(CHUNK, remaining));
      elapsed += CHUNK;
    }
  }

  async function speakScript(text, bypassAbort = false) {
    // Sanitize: strip any malformed [pause...] or [PAUSE...] markers that
    // wouldn't match our canonical regex. Prevents TTS from reading "bracket
    // pause bracket" aloud.
    const canonical = text.replace(/\[\s*pause[^\]]*\]/gi, (m) => {
      const num = m.match(/\d+/);
      return num ? `[PAUSE ${num[0]}]` : '';
    });

    const parts = canonical.split(/\[PAUSE\s+(\d+)\]/i);
    const display = $('textDisplay');
    for (let i = 0; i < parts.length; i++) {
      if (!bypassAbort && state.abortFlag) return;
      while (state.paused && !state.abortFlag) await sleep(200);
      if (!bypassAbort && state.abortFlag) return;
      if (i % 2 === 0) {
        const segment = parts[i].trim();
        if (!segment) continue;
        const chunks = segment.split(/(?<=[.!?])\s+/).filter(s => s.trim());
        for (const chunk of chunks) {
          if (!bypassAbort && state.abortFlag) return;
          while (state.paused && !state.abortFlag) await sleep(200);
          if (!bypassAbort && state.abortFlag) return;
          display.style.opacity = 0;
          await sleep(350);
          display.textContent = chunk;
          display.style.opacity = 0.5;
          if (drone.running && state.duckingEnabled) drone.duck();
          await speak(chunk);
          if (drone.running) drone.unduck();
        }
      } else {
        const seconds = parseInt(parts[i], 10) || 4;
        await interruptibleSleep(seconds * 1000, bypassAbort);
      }
    }
  }

  function speak(text) {
    return new Promise(resolve => {
      if (!('speechSynthesis' in window)) { setTimeout(resolve, text.length * 80); return; }
      // Always cancel before speaking to reset Chrome's internal state
      speechSynthesis.cancel();
      setTimeout(() => _doSpeak(text, resolve), 60);
    });
  }
  function _doSpeak(text, resolve) {
    const u = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);
    u.voice = state.voice || getSelectedVoice();
    u.rate = state.speechRate; u.pitch = state.voicePitch || 0.85; u.volume = state.voiceVolume ?? 1.0;
    let settled = false;
    let lastBoundaryAt = Date.now();
    const done = () => { if (!settled) { settled = true; clearInterval(silenceWatch); resolve(); } };
    u.onend = done;
    u.onerror = done;

    // Word-level highlighting via onboundary (Chrome/Safari desktop)
    const display = $('textDisplay');
    u.onboundary = (e) => {
      lastBoundaryAt = Date.now();
      if (e.name === 'word' && display) {
        const before = text.slice(0, e.charIndex);
        const word = text.slice(e.charIndex, e.charIndex + e.charLength);
        const after = text.slice(e.charIndex + e.charLength);
        display.innerHTML = `<span style="opacity:0.35">${escapeHtml(before)}</span><span style="opacity:1;color:var(--text)">${escapeHtml(word)}</span><span style="opacity:0.35">${escapeHtml(after)}</span>`;
      }
    };

    speechSynthesis.speak(u);

    // Double induction: fire a second utterance simultaneously
    if (state._doubleInduction && state._secondVoice) {
      const u2 = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);
      u2.voice = state._secondVoice;
      u2.rate = state.speechRate * 0.92; u2.pitch = 0.75; u2.volume = 0.7;
      u2.onend = () => {}; u2.onerror = () => {};
      speechSynthesis.speak(u2);
    }

    // ACTIVE SILENCE WATCHDOG — every 2s, check if speech has made progress.
    // If speaking but no onboundary fired in 5s, Chrome is stuck. Force-resolve.
    const silenceWatch = setInterval(() => {
      if (settled) { clearInterval(silenceWatch); return; }
      const silentFor = Date.now() - lastBoundaryAt;
      if (speechSynthesis.speaking && silentFor > 5000) {
        // Chrome is stuck — cancel and move on
        speechSynthesis.cancel();
        done();
      }
      if (!speechSynthesis.speaking && !speechSynthesis.pending) {
        // Speech finished without firing onend (Firefox edge case)
        done();
      }
    }, 2000);

    // Hard ceiling — absolute maximum wait per chunk (shorter than before)
    setTimeout(() => { speechSynthesis.cancel(); done(); }, Math.max(10000, text.length * 150));
  }
  const sleep = ms => new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, ms));

  // ====================================================================
  // AUDIO RECORDER (ambience-only — TTS can't be captured via Web Audio)
  // ====================================================================
  let _recorder = null, _recordedChunks = [];

  function startRecording() {
    if (!drone.ctx || !drone.master) { notify.warn('Start a session with a soundscape first.'); return; }
    try {
      const dest = drone.ctx.createMediaStreamDestination();
      drone.master.connect(dest);
      _recorder = new MediaRecorder(dest.stream, { mimeType: 'audio/webm;codecs=opus' });
      _recordedChunks = [];
      _recorder.ondataavailable = e => { if (e.data.size > 0) _recordedChunks.push(e.data); };
      _recorder.onstop = () => {
        if (_recordedChunks.length === 0) return;
        const blob = new Blob(_recordedChunks, { type: 'audio/webm' });
        const a = document.createElement('a');
        a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
        a.download = `stillness-ambience-${Date.now()}.webm`;
        a.click(); URL.revokeObjectURL(a.href);
        notify.success('Ambience recording downloaded.');
        _recordedChunks = [];
      };
      _recorder.start();
      notify.info('Recording ambience...');
      const btn = $('recordBtn');
      if (btn) { btn.textContent = '⏹ stop recording'; btn.classList.add('recording'); }
    } catch(e) { notify.error('Recording not supported in this browser.'); }
  }

  function stopRecording() {
    if (_recorder && _recorder.state === 'recording') {
      _recorder.stop(); _recorder = null;
      const btn = $('recordBtn');
      if (btn) { btn.textContent = '⏺ record ambience'; btn.classList.remove('recording'); }
    }
  }

  function toggleRecording() {
    if (_recorder && _recorder.state === 'recording') stopRecording();
    else startRecording();
  }

  async function finishSession(wasEmergency = false) {
    clearInterval(state._timeInterval);
    clearTimeout(state._safetyTimeout);
